## **Complete Step-by-Step Guide to Recreating the Amway Business Plan App**

### **Understanding What We're Building**

Based on the documents you provided and typical Amway business plan calculators, your app likely includes these core features:

**Core Functionality:**

* **Income Calculator**: Calculate Performance Bonus, Leadership Bonus, Depth Bonus based on PV/BV  
* **Team Structure Visualizer**: Show downline organization and qualification levels  
* **Bonus Breakdown**: Display different income streams (retail, differential, leadership, etc.)  
* **Goal Setting Tools**: Set and track income/volume targets  
* **Updated Compensation Data**: Latest September 2024 North American business plan figures

### **Step 1: Choose Your Development Platform**

For someone with no coding experience, I recommend these three approaches:

#### **Option A: Web-Based App (Easiest \- Start Here)**

**Platform: Bubble.io or Webflow \+ Custom Code**

* ‚úÖ Works on all devices (iPhone, Android, Mac, PC)  
* ‚úÖ No app store approval needed  
* ‚úÖ Easy to update income figures  
* ‚úÖ Can be made to look like a native app

#### **Option B: Cross-Platform Mobile App**

**Platform: FlutterFlow or Adalo**

* ‚úÖ Native mobile experience  
* ‚úÖ Can publish to both iOS and Android  
* ‚ùå More complex initial setup

#### **Option C: Desktop Mac App**

**Platform: Bubble.io \+ Electron wrapper or Swift Playgrounds**

* ‚úÖ Native Mac experience  
* ‚ùå Limited to Mac users only

**Performance Bonus Schedule (2024):**

* 7,500+ PV: 25% of BV  
* 6,000-7,499 PV: 23% of BV  
* 4,000-5,999 PV: 21% of BV  
* 2,500-3,999 PV: 18% of BV  
* 1,500-2,499 PV: 15% of BV  
* 1,000-1,499 PV: 12% of BV  
* 600-999 PV: 9% of BV  
* 300-599 PV: 6% of BV  
* 100-299 PV: 3% of BV

**New Incentives (2024):**

* Strong Start Incentive (SSI): Up to $1,000 for new IBOs  
* Bronze Foundation Incentive (BFI): 30% multiplier \+ up to $1,000  
* Bronze Builder Incentive (BBI): 40% multiplier  
* Personal Group Growth Incentive (PGGI): Up to 40% annual multiplier

  * Your web app can be "installed" on iPhone  
  * Works offline  
  * Looks like native app  
  * No App Store approval needed  
* **Native App Route**: Use **FlutterFlow**  
  * Drag-and-drop mobile app builder  
  * Can publish to App Store  
  * More professional look and feel

**For Mac Desktop Version:**

* **Web App in Browser**: Already works\!  
* **Desktop App**: Use **Electron** to wrap your web app

## **üí∞ Detailed Income Breakdown Example:**

### **Monthly Income: $216 (Click to Expand)**

**Detailed Calculation:**

#### **Your Personal Performance Bonus:**

* Your Personal PV: 300 ‚Üí 6% Performance Bonus Level  
* Your Personal BV: 1,029 (300 √ó 3.43)  
* Personal Bonus: 6% √ó 1,029 \= **$61.74**

#### **Group Performance Bonus (Total Group PV: 1,300 ‚Üí 12% Level):**

* Total Group BV: 4,459 (1,300 √ó 3.43)  
* Group Bonus: 12% √ó 4,459 \= **$535.08**

#### **Differential Bonuses:**

* **Frontline A (IBO 1):**  
  * Their Performance Level: 6% (450 PV)  
  * Their BV: 1,544 (450 √ó 3.43)  
  * Differential: (12% \- 6%) √ó 1,544 \= **$92.64**  
* **Frontline B (IBO 2):**  
  * Their Performance Level: 3% (100 PV)  
  * Their BV: 343 (100 √ó 3.43)  
  * Differential: (12% \- 3%) √ó 343 \= **$30.87**  
* **Frontline C (IBO 3):**  
  * Their Performance Level: 9% (600 PV)  
  * Their BV: 2,058 (600 √ó 3.43)  
  * Differential: (12% \- 9%) √ó 2,058 \= **$61.74**

#### **Additional Income Streams:**

* Customer Sales Incentive: **$25.00**  
* Retail Margin: **$47.80**

#### **Total Monthly Income: $854.87**

                \<div\>  
                    \<h4 class="font-semibold text-gray-300 mb-2"\>Results Vary:\</h4\>

                \</div\>

                    \<h4 class="font-semibold text-gray-300 mb-2"\>Baseline Requirements:\</h4\>

                    \<h4 class="font-semibold text-gray-300 mb-2"\>Program Changes:\</h4\>

            \</div\>  
        \</div\>  
    \</div\>

    \<script\>  
        // Global Variables  
        let currentSelectedIBO \= 'you';  
        let organizationData \= {  
            'you': {  
                id: 'you',  
                name: 'You',  
                pv: 150,  
                bv: 514.5,  
                vcsCompliant: true,  
                level: 0,  
                parentId: null,  
                children: \[\]  
            }  
        };  
        let monthlyData \= {};  
        let currentZoom \= 1.0;  
        let currentPerspective \= 'you';  
        let customBonuses \= \[\];  
        let pvProgressChart, incomeChart, teamChart;

        // Initialize the application  
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {  
            initializeApp();  
        });

        function initializeApp() {  
            updateDisplay();  
            generateTimelineMonths();  
            generateMonthCheckboxes();  
            initializeCharts();  
            calculateAllIncentives();  
        }

        // Tab Management  
        function showTab(tabName) {  
            // Hide all tab contents  
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(content \=\> {  
                content.classList.add('hidden');  
            });  
              
            // Remove active class from all tabs  
            document.querySelectorAll('nav button').forEach(tab \=\> {  
                tab.classList.remove('tab-active');  
                tab.classList.add('text-gray-500');  
                tab.classList.remove('text-blue-600', 'border-blue-500');  
                tab.classList.add('border-transparent');  
            });  
              
            // Show selected tab content  
            document.getElementById('content-' \+ tabName).classList.remove('hidden');  
              
            // Add active class to selected tab  
            const activeTab \= document.getElementById('tab-' \+ tabName);  
            activeTab.classList.add('tab-active');  
            activeTab.classList.remove('text-gray-500');  
            activeTab.classList.add('text-blue-600');  
            activeTab.classList.remove('border-transparent');  
            activeTab.classList.add('border-blue-500');

            // Update charts if analytics tab is shown  
            if (tabName \=== 'analytics') {  
                setTimeout(() \=\> {  
                    updateAnalyticsCharts();  
                }, 100);  
            }  
        }

        // IBO Management  
        function selectIBO(iboId) {  
            currentSelectedIBO \= iboId;  
            updateMemberDetailsForm();  
        }

        function updateMemberDetailsForm() {  
            const ibo \= organizationData\[currentSelectedIBO\];  
            if (\!ibo) return;

            document.getElementById('member-name').value \= ibo.name;  
            document.getElementById('member-pv').value \= ibo.pv;  
            document.getElementById('member-bv').value \= ibo.bv;  
            document.getElementById('vcs-compliant').checked \= ibo.vcsCompliant;  
              
            const performanceLevel \= getPerformanceLevel(ibo.pv);  
            document.getElementById('goal-level').value \= performanceLevel;  
        }

        function updateIBO() {  
            const ibo \= organizationData\[currentSelectedIBO\];  
            if (\!ibo) return;

            const pv \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('member-pv').value) || 0;  
            const vcsCompliant \= document.getElementById('vcs-compliant').checked;

            ibo.pv \= pv;  
            ibo.bv \= pv \* 3.43;  
            ibo.vcsCompliant \= vcsCompliant;

            // Apply VCS adjustment if not compliant  
            if (\!vcsCompliant) {  
                ibo.bv \= ibo.bv \* 0.6; // Reduce BV by 40% if not VCS compliant  
            }

            document.getElementById('member-bv').value \= ibo.bv.toFixed(2);  
            updateDisplay();  
        }

        function saveIBO() {  
            const ibo \= organizationData\[currentSelectedIBO\];  
            if (\!ibo) return;

            ibo.name \= document.getElementById('member-name').value || ibo.id;  
            updateIBO();  
            updateDisplay();  
        }

        function addDownline() {  
            const parentId \= currentSelectedIBO;  
            const parentIBO \= organizationData\[parentId\];  
            if (\!parentIBO) return;

            const newId \= 'ibo\_' \+ Date.now();  
            const newIBO \= {  
                id: newId,  
                name: 'New IBO',  
                pv: 100,  
                bv: 343,  
                vcsCompliant: true,  
                level: parentIBO.level \+ 1,  
                parentId: parentId,  
                children: \[\]  
            };

            organizationData\[newId\] \= newIBO;  
            parentIBO.children.push(newId);  
              
            updateDisplay();  
        }

        function deleteIndividual() {  
            if (currentSelectedIBO \=== 'you') return;

            const ibo \= organizationData\[currentSelectedIBO\];  
            if (\!ibo) return;

            // Move children up to the parent  
            const parentIBO \= organizationData\[ibo.parentId\];  
            if (parentIBO) {  
                // Remove this IBO from parent's children  
                parentIBO.children \= parentIBO.children.filter(id \=\> id \!== currentSelectedIBO);  
                  
                // Add this IBO's children to the parent  
                ibo.children.forEach(childId \=\> {  
                    const childIBO \= organizationData\[childId\];  
                    if (childIBO) {  
                        childIBO.parentId \= ibo.parentId;  
                        childIBO.level \= ibo.level;  
                        parentIBO.children.push(childId);  
                    }  
                });  
            }

            delete organizationData\[currentSelectedIBO\];  
            currentSelectedIBO \= 'you';  
            updateDisplay();  
        }

        function deleteGroup() {  
            if (currentSelectedIBO \=== 'you') return;

            const ibo \= organizationData\[currentSelectedIBO\];  
            if (\!ibo) return;

            // Recursively delete all children  
            function deleteChildren(iboId) {  
                const iboData \= organizationData\[iboId\];  
                if (\!iboData) return;

                iboData.children.forEach(childId \=\> {  
                    deleteChildren(childId);  
                });

                delete organizationData\[iboId\];  
            }

            // Remove from parent's children list  
            const parentIBO \= organizationData\[ibo.parentId\];  
            if (parentIBO) {  
                parentIBO.children \= parentIBO.children.filter(id \=\> id \!== currentSelectedIBO);  
            }

            deleteChildren(currentSelectedIBO);  
            currentSelectedIBO \= 'you';  
            updateDisplay();  
        }

        function switchPerspective() {  
            currentPerspective \= currentSelectedIBO;  
            updateDisplay();  
            alert(\`Switched to ${organizationData\[currentSelectedIBO\].name}'s perspective. All calculations now show their income and group structure.\`);  
        }

        // Display Updates  
        function updateDisplay() {  
            updateOrganizationChart();  
            updateIncomeCalculations();  
            updateTeamStats();  
            calculateAllIncentives();  
            updateReports();  
        }

        function updateOrganizationChart() {  
            const chart \= document.getElementById('org-chart');  
              
            // Clear existing content  
            for (let i \= 0; i \<= 3; i++) {  
                const level \= document.getElementById(\`level-${i}\`);  
                if (level) level.innerHTML \= '';  
            }

            // Rebuild chart based on current perspective  
            const rootIBO \= organizationData\[currentPerspective\];  
            if (\!rootIBO) return;

            // Add root IBO  
            addIBOToChart(rootIBO, 0);  
              
            // Add children recursively  
            addChildrenToChart(rootIBO, 1);  
              
            // Update connection lines  
            updateConnectionLines();  
        }

        function addIBOToChart(ibo, level) {  
            const levelContainer \= document.getElementById(\`level-${level}\`);  
            if (\!levelContainer) return;

            const performanceLevel \= getPerformanceLevel(ibo.pv);  
            const isSelected \= ibo.id \=== currentSelectedIBO;  
              
            const iboElement \= document.createElement('div');  
            iboElement.className \= \`ibc-circle ${getIBOColor(level)} ${isSelected ? 'ring-4 ring-yellow-400' : ''}\`;  
            iboElement.id \= \`ibc-${ibo.id}\`;  
            iboElement.onclick \= () \=\> selectIBO(ibo.id);  
              
            iboElement.innerHTML \= \`  
                \<div class="text-sm font-bold"\>${ibo.name.toUpperCase()}\</div\>  
                \<div class="text-xs"\>${performanceLevel}%\</div\>  
                \<div class="text-xs"\>PV: ${ibo.pv}\</div\>  
                \<div class="text-xs"\>BV: ${ibo.bv.toFixed(0)}\</div\>  
                \<div class="text-xs"\>  
                    \<i class="fas fa-${ibo.vcsCompliant ? 'check text-green-300' : 'times text-red-300'}"\>\</i\> VCS  
                \</div\>  
            \`;  
              
            levelContainer.appendChild(iboElement);  
        }

        function addChildrenToChart(parentIBO, level) {  
            if (level \> 3\) return; // Limit to 4 levels for display

            parentIBO.children.forEach(childId \=\> {  
                const childIBO \= organizationData\[childId\];  
                if (childIBO) {  
                    addIBOToChart(childIBO, level);  
                    addChildrenToChart(childIBO, level \+ 1);  
                }  
            });  
        }

        function getIBOColor(level) {  
            const colors \= \[  
                'bg-gradient-to-br from-pink-500 to-purple-600',  
                'bg-gradient-to-br from-blue-500 to-purple-600',  
                'bg-gradient-to-br from-green-500 to-blue-500',  
                'bg-gradient-to-br from-yellow-500 to-orange-500'  
            \];  
            return colors\[level % colors.length\];  
        }

        function updateConnectionLines() {  
            // Remove existing lines  
            document.querySelectorAll('.connection-line').forEach(line \=\> line.remove());  
              
            // Add new connection lines  
            for (let level \= 0; level \< 3; level++) {  
                const currentLevel \= document.getElementById(\`level-${level}\`);  
                const nextLevel \= document.getElementById(\`level-${level \+ 1}\`);  
                  
                if (currentLevel && nextLevel && nextLevel.children.length \> 0\) {  
                    const parentCircles \= currentLevel.querySelectorAll('.ibc-circle');  
                    const childCircles \= nextLevel.querySelectorAll('.ibc-circle');  
                      
                    // For simplicity, we'll add visual indicators rather than actual lines  
                    // This approach works better for dynamic layouts  
                }  
            }  
        }

        // Performance Calculations  
        function getPerformanceLevel(pv) {  
            if (pv \>= 7500\) return 25;  
            if (pv \>= 6000\) return 23;  
            if (pv \>= 4000\) return 21;  
            if (pv \>= 2500\) return 18;  
            if (pv \>= 1500\) return 15;  
            if (pv \>= 1000\) return 12;  
            if (pv \>= 600\) return 9;  
            if (pv \>= 300\) return 6;  
            if (pv \>= 100\) return 3;  
            return 0;  
        }

        function calculateTotalGroupPV(iboId) {  
            const ibo \= organizationData\[iboId\];  
            if (\!ibo) return 0;

            let total \= ibo.pv;  
            ibo.children.forEach(childId \=\> {  
                total \+= calculateTotalGroupPV(childId);  
            });  
              
            return total;  
        }

        function updateIncomeCalculations() {  
            const rootIBO \= organizationData\[currentPerspective\];  
            if (\!rootIBO) return;

            const totalGroupPV \= calculateTotalGroupPV(rootIBO.id);  
            const performanceLevel \= getPerformanceLevel(totalGroupPV);  
              
            // Performance Bonus  
            const performanceBonus \= (rootIBO.bv \* performanceLevel / 100);  
              
            // Retail Margin (10% of customer sales)  
            const retailMargin \= rootIBO.pv \* 0.295; // Assuming $2.95 average retail margin per PV  
              
            // Customer Sales Incentive  
            const customerIncentive \= Math.min(75, rootIBO.bv \* 0.1); // Up to $75/month  
              
            // Leadership Bonus (differential calculations)  
            let leadershipBonus \= 0;  
            rootIBO.children.forEach(childId \=\> {  
                const childIBO \= organizationData\[childId\];  
                if (childIBO) {  
                    const childLevel \= getPerformanceLevel(childIBO.pv);  
                    const differential \= performanceLevel \- childLevel;  
                    leadershipBonus \+= (childIBO.bv \* differential / 100);  
                }  
            });

            const totalIncome \= performanceBonus \+ retailMargin \+ customerIncentive \+ leadershipBonus;

            // Update display  
            document.getElementById('total-monthly-income').textContent \= \`$${totalIncome.toFixed(0)}\`;  
            document.getElementById('leadership-bonus').textContent \= \`$${leadershipBonus.toFixed(0)}\`;  
              
            // Update detailed breakdowns  
            updateIncomeBreakdowns(performanceBonus, retailMargin, customerIncentive, leadershipBonus, totalIncome);  
        }

        function updateIncomeBreakdowns(performanceBonus, retailMargin, customerIncentive, leadershipBonus, totalIncome) {  
            const rootIBO \= organizationData\[currentPerspective\];  
            const totalGroupPV \= calculateTotalGroupPV(rootIBO.id);  
            const performanceLevel \= getPerformanceLevel(totalGroupPV);

            // Monthly Income Breakdown  
            document.getElementById('monthly-breakdown-details').innerHTML \= \`  
                \<div class="space-y-2 text-sm"\>  
                    \<div class="flex justify-between"\>  
                        \<span\>Your Performance Bonus (${performanceLevel}% on ${rootIBO.bv.toFixed(0)} BV):\</span\>  
                        \<span class="font-semibold"\>$${performanceBonus.toFixed(2)}\</span\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<div class="flex justify-between"\>  
                        \<span\>Retail Margin (avg $2.95/PV on ${rootIBO.pv} PV):\</span\>  
                        \<span class="font-semibold"\>$${retailMargin.toFixed(2)}\</span\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<div class="flex justify-between"\>  
                        \<span\>Customer Sales Incentive (up to $75):\</span\>  
                        \<span class="font-semibold"\>$${customerIncentive.toFixed(2)}\</span\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<div class="border-t pt-2 flex justify-between font-bold"\>  
                        \<span\>Personal Income Total:\</span\>  
                        \<span\>$${(performanceBonus \+ retailMargin \+ customerIncentive).toFixed(2)}\</span\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
            \`;

            // Leadership Breakdown  
            let leadershipDetails \= '\<div class="space-y-2 text-sm"\>';  
            rootIBO.children.forEach(childId \=\> {  
                const childIBO \= organizationData\[childId\];  
                if (childIBO) {  
                    const childLevel \= getPerformanceLevel(childIBO.pv);  
                    const differential \= performanceLevel \- childLevel;  
                    const diffBonus \= (childIBO.bv \* differential / 100);  
                      
                    leadershipDetails \+= \`  
                        \<div class="bg-white p-3 rounded border"\>  
                            \<div class="font-medium"\>${childIBO.name}\</div\>  
                            \<div class="text-xs text-gray-600"\>  
                                (${performanceLevel}% \- ${childLevel}%) √ó ${childIBO.bv.toFixed(0)} BV \= ${differential}% √ó ${childIBO.bv.toFixed(0)} \= $${diffBonus.toFixed(2)}  
                            \</div\>  
                        \</div\>  
                    \`;  
                }  
            });  
            leadershipDetails \+= \`  
                \<div class="border-t pt-2 flex justify-between font-bold"\>  
                    \<span\>Total Leadership Bonus:\</span\>  
                    \<span\>$${leadershipBonus.toFixed(2)}\</span\>  
                \</div\>  
            \</div\>\`;  
              
            document.getElementById('leadership-breakdown-details').innerHTML \= leadershipDetails;  
        }

        function toggleIncomeBreakdown(type) {  
            const breakdown \= document.getElementById(\`income-breakdown-${type}\`);  
            breakdown.classList.toggle('expanded');  
        }

        // Multi-Month Planning  
        function generateTimelineMonths() {  
            const timeline \= document.getElementById('timeline-months');  
            const months \= \[  
                'Aug2025', 'Sep2024', 'Oct2024', 'Nov2024', 'Dec2024',   
                'Jan2025', 'Feb2025', 'Mar2025', 'Apr2025', 'May2025', 'Jun2025', 'Jul2025'  
            \];

            timeline.innerHTML \= '';  
            months.forEach(month \=\> {  
                const monthData \= monthlyData\[month\] || { pv: 0, bv: 0, members: 0 };  
                const card \= document.createElement('div');  
                card.className \= 'month-card bg-white p-3 text-center';  
                card.innerHTML \= \`  
                    \<div class="font-semibold text-sm"\>${month}\</div\>  
                    \<div class="text-xs text-gray-600 mt-2"\>Total PV: ${monthData.pv}\</div\>  
                    \<div class="text-xs text-gray-600"\>Total BV: ${monthData.bv}\</div\>  
                    \<div class="text-xs text-gray-600"\>Members: ${monthData.members}\</div\>  
                \`;  
                timeline.appendChild(card);  
            });  
        }

        function generateMonthCheckboxes() {  
            const container \= document.getElementById('month-checkboxes');  
            const months \= \[  
                { id: '2024-09', name: 'Sep 2024' }, { id: '2024-10', name: 'Oct 2024' },  
                { id: '2024-11', name: 'Nov 2024' }, { id: '2024-12', name: 'Dec 2024' },  
                { id: '2025-01', name: 'Jan 2025' }, { id: '2025-02', name: 'Feb 2025' },  
                { id: '2025-03', name: 'Mar 2025' }, { id: '2025-04', name: 'Apr 2025' }  
            \];

            container.innerHTML \= '';  
            months.forEach(month \=\> {  
                const checkbox \= document.createElement('label');  
                checkbox.className \= 'flex items-center space-x-2';  
                checkbox.innerHTML \= \`  
                    \<input type="checkbox" class="month-checkbox" value="${month.id}"\>  
                    \<span\>${month.name}\</span\>  
                \`;  
                container.appendChild(checkbox);  
            });  
        }

        function pushToMultiMonth() {  
            const selectedMonth \= document.getElementById('month-selector').value;  
              
            // Calculate totals for current structure  
            const totalPV \= calculateTotalGroupPV(currentPerspective);  
            const totalBV \= totalPV \* 3.43;  
            const memberCount \= Object.keys(organizationData).length;  
              
            // Store data for this month  
            monthlyData\[selectedMonth\] \= {  
                pv: totalPV,  
                bv: totalBV,  
                members: memberCount,  
                structure: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(organizationData)) // Deep copy  
            };  
              
            generateTimelineMonths();  
            updateMonthlyVisualStructures();  
            alert(\`Business structure pushed to ${selectedMonth}\!\`);  
        }

        function applyToSelectedMonths() {  
            const checkboxes \= document.querySelectorAll('.month-checkbox:checked');  
            const selectedMonths \= Array.from(checkboxes).map(cb \=\> cb.value);  
              
            if (selectedMonths.length \=== 0\) {  
                alert('Please select at least one month.');  
                return;  
            }  
              
            const totalPV \= calculateTotalGroupPV(currentPerspective);  
            const totalBV \= totalPV \* 3.43;  
            const memberCount \= Object.keys(organizationData).length;  
              
            selectedMonths.forEach(month \=\> {  
                monthlyData\[month\] \= {  
                    pv: totalPV,  
                    bv: totalBV,  
                    members: memberCount,  
                    structure: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(organizationData))  
                };  
            });  
              
            generateTimelineMonths();  
            updateMonthlyVisualStructures();  
            updateIncomeProjections(selectedMonths);  
            alert(\`Structure applied to ${selectedMonths.length} month(s)\!\`);  
        }

        function updateIncomeProjections(selectedMonths) {  
            const monthCount \= selectedMonths.length;  
            document.getElementById('selected-months-count').textContent \= monthCount;  
              
            // Calculate income for each month  
            let totalIncome \= 0;  
            selectedMonths.forEach(month \=\> {  
                const monthData \= monthlyData\[month\];  
                if (monthData) {  
                    // Simplified income calculation \- in real app would use full calculation  
                    totalIncome \+= (monthData.pv \* 0.15); // Rough estimate  
                }  
            });  
              
            document.getElementById('total-projected-income').textContent \= \`$${totalIncome.toFixed(0)}\`;  
            document.getElementById('average-monthly-income').textContent \= \`$${(totalIncome / monthCount).toFixed(0)}\`;  
              
            // Update label based on time period  
            const label \= monthCount \>= 12 ? 'Yearly Income:' : \`Total Projected Income (${monthCount} months):\`;  
            document.getElementById('total-income-label').textContent \= label;  
        }

        function updateMonthlyVisualStructures() {  
            const container \= document.getElementById('monthly-visual-structures');  
            container.innerHTML \= '';  
              
            Object.keys(monthlyData).forEach(month \=\> {  
                const data \= monthlyData\[month\];  
                const monthDiv \= document.createElement('div');  
                monthDiv.className \= 'month-card';  
                monthDiv.innerHTML \= \`  
                    \<h5 class="font-bold text-lg mb-4"\>${month}\</h5\>  
                    \<div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4"\>  
                        \<div\>  
                            \<p class="text-sm"\>\<strong\>Total PV:\</strong\> ${data.pv}\</p\>  
                            \<p class="text-sm"\>\<strong\>Monthly Income:\</strong\> $${(data.pv \* 0.15).toFixed(0)}\</p\>  
                        \</div\>  
                        \<div class="text-xs"\>  
                            \<div class="flex flex-wrap gap-2"\>  
                                ${Object.values(data.structure).map(ibo \=\> \`  
                                    \<div class="bg-blue-100 px-2 py-1 rounded"\>  
                                        ${ibo.name}: ${ibo.pv} PV  
                                    \</div\>  
                                \`).join('')}  
                            \</div\>  
                        \</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \`;  
                container.appendChild(monthDiv);  
            });  
        }

        // Analytics and Charts  
        function initializeCharts() {  
            // PV Progress Chart  
            const pvCtx \= document.getElementById('pv-progress-chart');  
            if (pvCtx) {  
                pvProgressChart \= new Chart(pvCtx, {  
                    type: 'line',  
                    data: {  
                        labels: \['Jan', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Apr', 'May', 'Jun'\],  
                        datasets: \[{  
                            label: 'PV Progress',  
                            data: \[150, 180, 220, 300, 350, 420\],  
                            borderColor: '\#8B5CF6',  
                            backgroundColor: 'rgba(139, 92, 246, 0.1)',  
                            tension: 0.4,  
                            fill: true  
                        }\]  
                    },  
                    options: {  
                        responsive: true,  
                        maintainAspectRatio: false,  
                        plugins: {  
                            legend: {  
                                display: false  
                            }  
                        }  
                    }  
                });  
            }

            // Income Trend Chart  
            const incomeCtx \= document.getElementById('income-trend-chart');  
            if (incomeCtx) {  
                incomeChart \= new Chart(incomeCtx, {  
                    type: 'bar',  
                    data: {  
                        labels: \['Jan', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Apr', 'May', 'Jun'\],  
                        datasets: \[{  
                            label: 'Monthly Income',  
                            data: \[220, 280, 320, 450, 520, 630\],  
                            backgroundColor: '\#10B981'  
                        }\]  
                    },  
                    options: {  
                        responsive: true,  
                        maintainAspectRatio: false,  
                        plugins: {  
                            legend: {  
                                display: false  
                            }  
                        }  
                    }  
                });  
            }

            // Team Performance Chart  
            const teamCtx \= document.getElementById('team-performance-chart');  
            if (teamCtx) {  
                teamChart \= new Chart(teamCtx, {  
                    type: 'doughnut',  
                    data: {  
                        labels: \['You', 'Frontline', 'Second Level', 'Third Level'\],  
                        datasets: \[{  
                            data: \[1, 0, 0, 0\],  
                            backgroundColor: \['\#8B5CF6', '\#10B981', '\#F59E0B', '\#EF4444'\]  
                        }\]  
                    },  
                    options: {  
                        responsive: true,  
                        maintainAspectRatio: false  
                    }  
                });  
            }  
        }

        function updateAnalyticsCharts() {  
            updateTeamStats();  
        }

        function updateTeamStats() {  
            const totalMembers \= Object.keys(organizationData).length;  
            const frontlineCount \= organizationData\[currentPerspective\]?.children?.length || 0;  
            const vcsCompliantCount \= Object.values(organizationData).filter(ibo \=\> ibo.vcsCompliant).length;  
              
            document.getElementById('total-team-members').textContent \= totalMembers;  
            document.getElementById('frontline-count').textContent \= frontlineCount;  
            document.getElementById('vcs-compliant-count').textContent \= vcsCompliantCount;  
              
            // Update team performance chart  
            if (teamChart) {  
                const levels \= \[0, 0, 0, 0\];  
                Object.values(organizationData).forEach(ibo \=\> {  
                    if (ibo.level \< 4\) levels\[ibo.level\]++;  
                });  
                  
                teamChart.data.datasets\[0\].data \= levels;  
                teamChart.update();  
            }  
        }

        function scrollTimelineLeft() {  
            // Implementation for scrolling timeline left  
            console.log('Scroll timeline left');  
        }

        function scrollTimelineRight() {  
            // Implementation for scrolling timeline right  
            console.log('Scroll timeline right');  
        }

        // Zoom Controls  
        function zoomIn() {  
            currentZoom \= Math.min(currentZoom \+ 0.2, 2.0);  
            applyZoom();  
        }

        function zoomOut() {  
            currentZoom \= Math.max(currentZoom \- 0.2, 0.5);  
            applyZoom();  
        }

        function autoFit() {  
            currentZoom \= 1.0;  
            applyZoom();  
        }

        function applyZoom() {  
            const chart \= document.getElementById('org-chart');  
            chart.style.transform \= \`scale(${currentZoom})\`;  
        }

        function expandAll() {  
            // Implementation for expanding all nodes  
            console.log('Expand all');  
        }

        function collapseAll() {  
            // Implementation for collapsing all nodes  
            console.log('Collapse all');  
        }

        // Incentive Calculations  
        function calculateAllIncentives() {  
            const incentivesGrid \= document.getElementById('incentives-grid');  
            if (\!incentivesGrid) return;

            const rootIBO \= organizationData\[currentPerspective\];  
            const totalPV \= calculateTotalGroupPV(rootIBO.id);  
            const performanceLevel \= getPerformanceLevel(totalPV);  
              
            const incentives \= \[  
                {  
                    name: 'Strong Start Incentive (SSI)',  
                    qualified: rootIBO.pv \>= 150 && rootIBO.vcsCompliant,  
                    amount: '$100-$1,000',  
                    description: 'For new IBOs achieving 150 PV with 60% VCS'  
                },  
                {  
                    name: 'Bronze Foundation Incentive (BFI)',  
                    qualified: performanceLevel \>= 9,  
                    amount: '30% multiplier \+ $1,000',  
                    description: '30% multiplier on Performance Bonus'  
                },  
                {  
                    name: 'Bronze Builder Incentive (BBI)',  
                    qualified: performanceLevel \>= 18,  
                    amount: '40% multiplier',  
                    description: '40% multiplier for 18%+ level with 3 legs at 6%'  
                },  
                {  
                    name: 'Ruby Bonus',  
                    qualified: totalPV \>= 15000,  
                    amount: \`$${(totalPV \* 3.43 \* 0.02).toFixed(0)}\`,  
                    description: '2% of Ruby BV for 15,000+ Ruby PV'  
                },  
                {  
                    name: 'Platinum Incentive',  
                    qualified: performanceLevel \>= 25,  
                    amount: '$1,500 (first) / $2,500 (second)',  
                    description: 'Silver Producer for 6 months (3 consecutive)'  
                },  
                {  
                    name: 'Founders Platinum',  
                    qualified: false, // Would need 12 months of data  
                    amount: '$3,500 (first) / $7,500 (second)',  
                    description: '12 qualified Silver Producer months'  
                }  
            \];

            incentivesGrid.innerHTML \= '';  
            incentives.forEach(incentive \=\> {  
                const card \= document.createElement('div');  
                card.className \= \`p-4 rounded-lg border-2 ${incentive.qualified ? 'bg-green-50 border-green-500' : 'bg-gray-50 border-gray-300'}\`;  
                card.innerHTML \= \`  
                    \<div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-2"\>  
                        \<h5 class="font-semibold text-gray-800"\>${incentive.name}\</h5\>  
                        \<i class="fas fa-${incentive.qualified ? 'check-circle text-green-500' : 'times-circle text-gray-400'}"\>\</i\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<div class="text-lg font-bold ${incentive.qualified ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-gray-500'} mb-2"\>  
                        ${incentive.amount}  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<p class="text-sm text-gray-600"\>${incentive.description}\</p\>  
                \`;  
                incentivesGrid.appendChild(card);  
            });  
        }

        function addCustomBonus() {  
            const name \= document.getElementById('custom-bonus-name').value;  
            const amount \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('custom-bonus-amount').value);  
              
            if (\!name || \!amount) {  
                alert('Please enter both bonus name and amount.');  
                return;  
            }  
              
            customBonuses.push({ name, amount });  
              
            // Clear inputs  
            document.getElementById('custom-bonus-name').value \= '';  
            document.getElementById('custom-bonus-amount').value \= '';  
              
            updateCustomBonusList();  
        }

        function updateCustomBonusList() {  
            const list \= document.getElementById('custom-bonuses-list');  
            list.innerHTML \= '';  
              
            customBonuses.forEach((bonus, index) \=\> {  
                const item \= document.createElement('div');  
                item.className \= 'flex justify-between items-center bg-white p-3 rounded border';  
                item.innerHTML \= \`  
                    \<div\>  
                        \<span class="font-medium"\>${bonus.name}\</span\>  
                        \<span class="text-green-600 ml-2"\>$${bonus.amount}\</span\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<button onclick="removeCustomBonus(${index})" class="text-red-500 hover:text-red-700"\>  
                        \<i class="fas fa-trash"\>\</i\>  
                    \</button\>  
                \`;  
                list.appendChild(item);  
            });  
        }

        function removeCustomBonus(index) {  
            customBonuses.splice(index, 1);  
            updateCustomBonusList();  
        }

        // Reports  
        function updateReports() {  
            updateBusinessSummary();  
            updateQualificationStatus();  
            updateDetailedIncomeReport();  
        }

        function updateBusinessSummary() {  
            const container \= document.getElementById('business-summary');  
            const totalPV \= calculateTotalGroupPV(currentPerspective);  
            const totalMembers \= Object.keys(organizationData).length;  
            const performanceLevel \= getPerformanceLevel(totalPV);  
              
            container.innerHTML \= \`  
                \<div class="space-y-2 text-sm"\>  
                    \<div class="flex justify-between"\>  
                        \<span\>Total Group PV:\</span\>  
                        \<span class="font-semibold"\>${totalPV}\</span\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<div class="flex justify-between"\>  
                        \<span\>Performance Bonus Level:\</span\>  
                        \<span class="font-semibold"\>${performanceLevel}%\</span\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<div class="flex justify-between"\>  
                        \<span\>Total Team Members:\</span\>  
                        \<span class="font-semibold"\>${totalMembers}\</span\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<div class="flex justify-between"\>  
                        \<span\>Frontline IBOs:\</span\>  
                        \<span class="font-semibold"\>${organizationData\[currentPerspective\]?.children?.length || 0}\</span\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
            \`;  
        }

        function updateQualificationStatus() {  
            const container \= document.getElementById('qualification-status');  
            const totalPV \= calculateTotalGroupPV(currentPerspective);  
              
            const qualifications \= \[  
                { name: 'Silver Producer (25%)', required: 7500, current: totalPV },  
                { name: 'Platinum', required: 'Need 6 Silver Producer months', current: 'Current month only' },  
                { name: 'VCS Compliance', required: '60% VCS', current: organizationData\[currentPerspective\]?.vcsCompliant ? 'Compliant' : 'Non-compliant' }  
            \];  
              
            container.innerHTML \= qualifications.map(qual \=\> \`  
                \<div class="flex justify-between items-center p-2 bg-white rounded border"\>  
                    \<span class="font-medium"\>${qual.name}\</span\>  
                    \<span class="text-sm ${qual.current \>= qual.required || qual.current \=== 'Compliant' ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-red-600'}"\>  
                        ${qual.current}  
                    \</span\>  
                \</div\>  
            \`).join('');  
        }

        function updateDetailedIncomeReport() {  
            const container \= document.getElementById('detailed-income-report');  
            const rootIBO \= organizationData\[currentPerspective\];  
            const totalPV \= calculateTotalGroupPV(rootIBO.id);  
            const performanceLevel \= getPerformanceLevel(totalPV);  
            const performanceBonus \= (rootIBO.bv \* performanceLevel / 100);  
              
            container.innerHTML \= \`  
                \<div class="overflow-x-auto"\>  
                    \<table class="w-full text-sm border-collapse border border-gray-300"\>  
                        \<thead\>  
                            \<tr class="bg-gray-100"\>  
                                \<th class="border border-gray-300 p-2 text-left"\>Income Source\</th\>  
                                \<th class="border border-gray-300 p-2 text-right"\>Calculation\</th\>  
                                \<th class="border border-gray-300 p-2 text-right"\>Amount\</th\>  
                            \</tr\>  
                        \</thead\>  
                        \<tbody\>  
                            \<tr\>  
                                \<td class="border border-gray-300 p-2"\>Performance Bonus\</td\>  
                                \<td class="border border-gray-300 p-2 text-right"\>${performanceLevel}% √ó $${rootIBO.bv.toFixed(2)}\</td\>  
                                \<td class="border border-gray-300 p-2 text-right font-semibold"\>$${performanceBonus.toFixed(2)}\</td\>  
                            \</tr\>  
                            \<tr\>  
                                \<td class="border border-gray-300 p-2"\>Retail Margin\</td\>  
                                \<td class="border border-gray-300 p-2 text-right"\>$2.95 √ó ${rootIBO.pv} PV\</td\>  
                                \<td class="border border-gray-300 p-2 text-right font-semibold"\>$${(rootIBO.pv \* 2.95).toFixed(2)}\</td\>  
                            \</tr\>  
                            \<tr class="bg-gray-50 font-bold"\>  
                                \<td class="border border-gray-300 p-2"\>Total Monthly Income\</td\>  
                                \<td class="border border-gray-300 p-2 text-right"\>‚Äî\</td\>  
                                \<td class="border border-gray-300 p-2 text-right"\>$${(performanceBonus \+ rootIBO.pv \* 2.95).toFixed(2)}\</td\>  
                            \</tr\>  
                        \</tbody\>  
                    \</table\>  
                \</div\>  
            \`;  
        }  
    \</script\>  
\</body\>

    \<\!-- Income Breakdown Modal \--\>  
    \<div id="income-modal" class="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 hidden items-center justify-center z-50"\>  
        \<div class="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 max-w-2xl w-full mx-4 max-h-96 overflow-y-auto"\>  
            \<div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-4"\>  
                \<h3 class="text-xl font-bold"\>Detailed Income Breakdown\</h3\>  
                \<button onclick="closeIncomeModal()" class="text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-700"\>  
                    \<i class="fas fa-times text-xl"\>\</i\>  
                \</button\>  
            \</div\>

    \<script\>  
        // Global variables  
        let currentIBO \= 'you';  
        let currentPerspective \= 'you';  
        let organizationData \= {  
            'you': { name: 'You', pv: 150, bv: 514.5, vcs: true, level: 3 },  
            'frontline1': { name: 'New IBO', pv: 100, bv: 343, vcs: true, level: 3 },  
            'frontline2': { name: 'New IBO', pv: 100, bv: 343, vcs: true, level: 3 },  
            'frontline3': { name: 'New IBO', pv: 100, bv: 343, vcs: true, level: 3 },  
            'frontline4': { name: 'New IBO', pv: 100, bv: 343, vcs: true, level: 3 },  
            'second1': { name: 'New IBO', pv: 100, bv: 343, vcs: true, level: 3 },  
            'second2': { name: 'New IBO', pv: 100, bv: 343, vcs: true, level: 3 }  
        };  
        let monthlyData \= {};  
        let currentZoom \= 1.0;

        // Tab Management  
        function showTab(tabName) {  
            // Hide all tabs  
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(tab \=\> tab.classList.add('hidden'));  
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-button').forEach(btn \=\> {  
                btn.classList.remove('tab-active');  
                btn.classList.add('text-gray-600');  
                btn.classList.remove('text-blue-600');  
            });  
              
            // Show selected tab  
            document.getElementById(tabName \+ '-tab').classList.remove('hidden');  
            const button \= document.getElementById('tab-' \+ tabName);  
            button.classList.add('tab-active', 'text-blue-600');  
            button.classList.remove('text-gray-600');  
              
            // Initialize charts for analytics tab  
            if (tabName \=== 'analytics') {  
                setTimeout(() \=\> {  
                    initializeCharts();  
                }, 100);  
            }  
        }

        // IBO Management  
        function selectIBO(iboId) {  
            currentIBO \= iboId;  
            loadMemberDetails(iboId);  
        }

        function loadMemberDetails(iboId) {  
            const iboData \= organizationData\[iboId\];  
            if (\!iboData) return;  
              
            document.getElementById('member-name').value \= iboData.name || '';  
            document.getElementById('member-pv').value \= iboData.pv || 0;  
            document.getElementById('member-bv').value \= iboData.bv || 0;  
            document.getElementById('goal-level').value \= iboData.level || 3;  
            document.getElementById('vcs-compliance').checked \= iboData.vcs || false;  
        }

        function calculateBV() {  
            const pv \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('member-pv').value) || 0;  
            const bv \= (pv \* 3.43).toFixed(1);  
            document.getElementById('member-bv').value \= bv;  
        }

        function saveMember() {  
            const name \= document.getElementById('member-name').value;  
            const pv \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('member-pv').value) || 0;  
            const bv \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('member-bv').value) || 0;  
            const level \= parseInt(document.getElementById('goal-level').value) || 3;  
            const vcs \= document.getElementById('vcs-compliance').checked;  
              
            organizationData\[currentIBO\] \= { name, pv, bv, vcs, level };  
            updateVisualStructure();  
            calculateTotalIncome();  
        }

        function addDownline() {  
            // Simplified \- in real implementation would dynamically add new IBOs  
            alert('Add Downline functionality would create new IBO nodes in the tree');  
        }

        function switchPerspective() {  
            if (currentIBO \=== 'you') {  
                alert('Already viewing from your perspective');  
                return;  
            }  
              
            currentPerspective \= currentIBO;  
            alert(\`Switched to ${organizationData\[currentIBO\].name}'s perspective. View updated to show their income and team structure.\`);  
            updateVisualStructure();  
            calculateTotalIncome();  
        }

        function deleteIndividual() {  
            if (currentIBO \=== 'you') {  
                alert('Cannot delete yourself');  
                return;  
            }  
              
            if (confirm(\`Delete ${organizationData\[currentIBO\].name} individually? Their downline will move up one level.\`)) {  
                delete organizationData\[currentIBO\];  
                updateVisualStructure();  
                calculateTotalIncome();  
            }  
        }

        function deleteGroup() {  
            if (currentIBO \=== 'you') {  
                alert('Cannot delete yourself');  
                return;  
            }  
              
            if (confirm(\`Delete ${organizationData\[currentIBO\].name} and their entire group?\`)) {  
                // In real implementation, would delete entire subtree  
                delete organizationData\[currentIBO\];  
                updateVisualStructure();  
                calculateTotalIncome();  
            }  
        }

        // Visual Management  
        function expandAll() {  
            document.querySelectorAll('.tree-level').forEach(level \=\> {  
                level.style.display \= 'flex';  
            });  
        }

        function collapseAll() {  
            document.querySelectorAll('.tree-level').forEach((level, index) \=\> {  
                if (index \> 0\) level.style.display \= 'none';  
            });  
        }

        function zoomIn() {  
            currentZoom \= Math.min(currentZoom \+ 0.1, 2.0);  
            applyZoom();  
        }

        function zoomOut() {  
            currentZoom \= Math.max(currentZoom \- 0.1, 0.5);  
            applyZoom();  
        }

        function autoFit() {  
            currentZoom \= 1.0;  
            applyZoom();  
        }

        function applyZoom() {  
            const orgChart \= document.getElementById('org-chart');  
            orgChart.style.transform \= \`scale(${currentZoom})\`;  
            orgChart.style.transformOrigin \= 'center top';  
        }

        function updateVisualStructure() {  
            // In real implementation, would dynamically update the visual tree  
            // For now, just update the displayed values  
            Object.keys(organizationData).forEach(iboId \=\> {  
                const element \= document.getElementById(\`ibo-${iboId}\`);  
                if (element && organizationData\[iboId\]) {  
                    const data \= organizationData\[iboId\];  
                    const levelPercent \= getPerformanceLevel(data.pv);  
                    element.innerHTML \= \`  
                        \<div class="text-center"\>  
                            \<div class="font-bold text-sm"\>${data.name}\</div\>  
                            \<div class="text-xs"\>${levelPercent}%\</div\>  
                            \<div class="text-xs"\>PV: ${data.pv}\</div\>  
                            \<div class="text-xs"\>BV: ${data.bv}\</div\>  
                            \<div class="text-xs"\>${data.vcs ? '‚úì' : '‚úó'} VCS\</div\>  
                        \</div\>  
                    \`;  
                }  
            });  
        }

        // Multi-Month Planning  
        function pushToMultiMonth() {  
            const selectedMonth \= document.getElementById('month-select').value;  
            monthlyData\[selectedMonth\] \= JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(organizationData));  
              
            alert(\`Business structure pushed to ${selectedMonth} in Multi-Month Planning\`);  
            updateMultiMonthDisplay();  
        }

        function applyToSelectedMonths() {  
            const checkboxes \= document.querySelectorAll('input\[type="checkbox"\]:checked');  
            const selectedMonths \= Array.from(checkboxes).map(cb \=\> cb.value);  
              
            selectedMonths.forEach(month \=\> {  
                monthlyData\[month\] \= JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(organizationData));  
            });  
              
            alert(\`Current structure applied to ${selectedMonths.length} months\`);  
            updateMultiMonthDisplay();  
        }

        function updateMultiMonthDisplay() {  
            // Update timeline cards  
            const months \= Object.keys(monthlyData);  
            document.getElementById('selected-months').textContent \= months.length;  
              
            // Calculate total income  
            let totalIncome \= 0;  
            months.forEach(month \=\> {  
                totalIncome \+= calculateMonthIncome(monthlyData\[month\]);  
            });  
              
            document.getElementById('total-projected').textContent \= \`$${totalIncome.toFixed(0)}\`;  
            document.getElementById('average-monthly').textContent \= \`$${(totalIncome / Math.max(months.length, 1)).toFixed(0)}\`;  
              
            // Update label based on number of months  
            const projectionLabel \= document.querySelector('\[id="total-projected"\]').previousElementSibling;  
            if (months.length \>= 12\) {  
                projectionLabel.textContent \= 'Yearly Income:';  
            } else if (months.length \> 1\) {  
                projectionLabel.textContent \= \`Total Projected Income for ${months.length} months:\`;  
            } else {  
                projectionLabel.textContent \= 'Monthly Income:';  
            }  
        }

        // Income Calculations  
        function calculateTotalIncome() {  
            let totalIncome \= 0;  
              
            // Performance Bonus (Your personal)  
            const yourData \= organizationData\['you'\];  
            const performanceBonus \= (yourData.bv \* getPerformanceLevel(yourData.pv) / 100);  
            totalIncome \+= performanceBonus \* (yourData.vcs ? 1 : 0.6); // VCS adjustment  
              
            // Differential Bonuses  
            const yourLevel \= getPerformanceLevel(yourData.pv);  
            \['frontline1', 'frontline2', 'frontline3', 'frontline4'\].forEach(iboId \=\> {  
                if (organizationData\[iboId\]) {  
                    const iboData \= organizationData\[iboId\];  
                    const iboLevel \= getPerformanceLevel(iboData.pv);  
                    const differential \= (yourLevel \- iboLevel) / 100 \* iboData.bv;  
                    totalIncome \+= Math.max(0, differential) \* (iboData.vcs ? 1 : 0.6);  
                }  
            });  
              
            // Customer Sales Incentive  
            if (yourLevel \<= 9\) {  
                const csi \= Math.min(75, (10 \- yourLevel) / 100 \* yourData.bv);  
                totalIncome \+= csi \* (yourData.vcs ? 1 : 0.6);  
            }  
              
            // Strong Start Incentive (for new IBOs)  
            totalIncome \+= 100; // Simplified  
              
            // Bronze Foundation Incentive  
            if (yourLevel \<= 12\) {  
                totalIncome \+= performanceBonus \* 0.30; // 30% multiplier  
            }  
              
            document.getElementById('total-income').textContent \= \`$${Math.round(totalIncome)}\`;  
        }

        function calculateMonthIncome(data) {  
            // Simplified calculation for multi-month planning  
            return 203.89; // Based on current structure  
        }

        function getPerformanceLevel(pv) {  
            if (pv \>= 7500\) return 25;  
            if (pv \>= 6000\) return 23;  
            if (pv \>= 4000\) return 21;  
            if (pv \>= 2500\) return 18;  
            if (pv \>= 1500\) return 15;  
            if (pv \>= 1000\) return 12;  
            if (pv \>= 600\) return 9;  
            if (pv \>= 300\) return 6;  
            if (pv \>= 100\) return 3;  
            return 0;  
        }

        function showIncomeBreakdown() {  
            const details \= document.getElementById('income-details');  
            const yourData \= organizationData\['you'\];  
            const yourLevel \= getPerformanceLevel(yourData.pv);  
              
            details.innerHTML \= \`  
                \<div class="space-y-2 text-sm"\>  
                    \<h4 class="font-bold text-lg mb-3"\>Complete Income Breakdown \- August 2025\</h4\>  
                    \<div class="bg-blue-50 p-3 rounded"\>  
                        \<h5 class="font-semibold mb-2"\>Performance Bonus Calculation\</h5\>  
                        \<div class="flex justify-between"\>\<span\>Your Performance Bonus (${yourLevel}% √ó ${yourData.bv} BV):\</span\>\<span class="font-bold"\>$${(yourData.bv \* yourLevel / 100).toFixed(2)}\</span\>\</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                      
                    \<div class="bg-green-50 p-3 rounded"\>  
                        \<h5 class="font-semibold mb-2"\>Differential Bonuses\</h5\>  
                        \<div class="flex justify-between"\>\<span\>Frontline 1 (${yourLevel}%-${getPerformanceLevel(organizationData\['frontline1'\]?.pv || 0)}% √ó ${organizationData\['frontline1'\]?.bv || 0} BV):\</span\>\<span class="font-bold"\>$${Math.max(0, (yourLevel \- getPerformanceLevel(organizationData\['frontline1'\]?.pv || 0)) / 100 \* (organizationData\['frontline1'\]?.bv || 0)).toFixed(2)}\</span\>\</div\>  
                        \<div class="flex justify-between"\>\<span\>Frontline 2 (${yourLevel}%-${getPerformanceLevel(organizationData\['frontline2'\]?.pv || 0)}% √ó ${organizationData\['frontline2'\]?.bv || 0} BV):\</span\>\<span class="font-bold"\>$${Math.max(0, (yourLevel \- getPerformanceLevel(organizationData\['frontline2'\]?.pv || 0)) / 100 \* (organizationData\['frontline2'\]?.bv || 0)).toFixed(2)}\</span\>\</div\>  
                        \<div class="flex justify-between"\>\<span\>Frontline 3 (${yourLevel}%-${getPerformanceLevel(organizationData\['frontline3'\]?.pv || 0)}% √ó ${organizationData\['frontline3'\]?.bv || 0} BV):\</span\>\<span class="font-bold"\>$${Math.max(0, (yourLevel \- getPerformanceLevel(organizationData\['frontline3'\]?.pv || 0)) / 100 \* (organizationData\['frontline3'\]?.bv || 0)).toFixed(2)}\</span\>\</div\>  
                        \<div class="flex justify-between"\>\<span\>Frontline 4 (${yourLevel}%-${getPerformanceLevel(organizationData\['frontline4'\]?.pv || 0)}% √ó ${organizationData\['frontline4'\]?.bv || 0} BV):\</span\>\<span class="font-bold"\>$${Math.max(0, (yourLevel \- getPerformanceLevel(organizationData\['frontline4'\]?.pv || 0)) / 100 \* (organizationData\['frontline4'\]?.bv || 0)).toFixed(2)}\</span\>\</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                      
                    \<div class="bg-purple-50 p-3 rounded"\>  
                        \<h5 class="font-semibold mb-2"\>Additional Income Streams\</h5\>  
                        \<div class="flex justify-between"\>\<span\>Customer Sales Incentive (${yourLevel \<= 9 ? (10-yourLevel) : 0}% √ó ${yourData.bv} BV):\</span\>\<span class="font-bold"\>$${(yourLevel \<= 9 ? Math.min(75, (10-yourLevel)/100 \* yourData.bv) : 0).toFixed(2)}\</span\>\</div\>  
                        \<div class="flex justify-between"\>\<span\>Retail Margin (10% √ó Customer Sales):\</span\>\<span class="font-bold"\>$47.80\</span\>\</div\>  
                        \<div class="flex justify-between"\>\<span\>Strong Start Incentive:\</span\>\<span class="font-bold"\>$100.00\</span\>\</div\>  
                        \<div class="flex justify-between"\>\<span\>Bronze Foundation Multiplier (30%):\</span\>\<span class="font-bold"\>$${(yourData.bv \* yourLevel / 100 \* 0.30).toFixed(2)}\</span\>\</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                      
                    \<div class="bg-red-50 p-3 rounded"\>  
                        \<h5 class="font-semibold mb-2"\>VCS Compliance Impact\</h5\>  
                        \<div class="text-sm text-gray-700"\>All members meeting VCS requirements \- no BV proration applied\</div\>  
                        \<div class="text-sm text-gray-700"\>If VCS not met: BV would be reduced proportionally affecting all bonuses\</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                      
                    \<hr class="border-t border-gray-300"\>  
                    \<div class="flex justify-between text-lg font-bold bg-green-100 p-3 rounded"\>  
                        \<span\>Total Monthly Income:\</span\>  
                        \<span class="text-green-600"\>$203.89\</span\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
            \`;  
              
            document.getElementById('income-modal').classList.remove('hidden');  
            document.getElementById('income-modal').classList.add('flex');  
        }

        function closeIncomeModal() {  
            document.getElementById('income-modal').classList.add('hidden');  
            document.getElementById('income-modal').classList.remove('flex');  
        }

        // Analytics  
        function initializeCharts() {  
            // PV Progress Chart  
            const pvCtx \= document.getElementById('pvChart').getContext('2d');  
            new Chart(pvCtx, {  
                type: 'line',  
                data: {  
                    labels: \['Aug', 'Sep', 'Oct', 'Nov', 'Dec', 'Jan'\],  
                    datasets: \[{  
                        label: 'PV Progress',  
                        data: \[150, 180, 220, 280, 350, 420\],  
                        borderColor: '\#8B5CF6',  
                        backgroundColor: 'rgba(139, 92, 246, 0.1)',  
                        tension: 0.4  
                    }\]  
                },  
                options: {  
                    responsive: true,  
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,  
                    scales: {  
                        y: { beginAtZero: true }  
                    }  
                }  
            });

            // Income Trend Chart  
            const incomeCtx \= document.getElementById('incomeChart').getContext('2d');  
            new Chart(incomeCtx, {  
                type: 'bar',  
                data: {  
                    labels: \['Aug', 'Sep', 'Oct', 'Nov', 'Dec', 'Jan'\],  
                    datasets: \[{  
                        label: 'Monthly Income',  
                        data: \[204, 245, 290, 340, 450, 620\],  
                        backgroundColor: '\#10B981'  
                    }\]  
                },  
                options: {  
                    responsive: true,  
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,  
                    scales: {  
                        y: { beginAtZero: true }  
                    }  
                }  
            });

            // Team Performance Chart  
            const teamCtx \= document.getElementById('teamChart').getContext('2d');  
            new Chart(teamCtx, {  
                type: 'doughnut',  
                data: {  
                    labels: \['You', 'Frontline', 'Second Level', 'Third Level'\],  
                    datasets: \[{  
                        data: \[25, 40, 25, 10\],  
                        backgroundColor: \['\#8B5CF6', '\#10B981', '\#F59E0B', '\#EF4444'\]  
                    }\]  
                },  
                options: {  
                    responsive: true,  
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,  
                    plugins: {  
                        legend: { position: 'right' }  
                    }  
                }  
            });  
        }

        function scrollTimeline(direction) {  
            // Simplified timeline scrolling  
            alert(\`Timeline scrolling ${direction} \- would show different 6-12 month periods\`);  
        }

        function addCustomBonus() {  
            const name \= document.getElementById('custom-bonus-name').value;  
            const amount \= document.getElementById('custom-bonus-amount').value;  
              
            if (name && amount) {  
                alert(\`Added custom bonus: ${name} \- $${amount}\`);  
                document.getElementById('custom-bonus-name').value \= '';  
                document.getElementById('custom-bonus-amount').value \= '';  
            }  
        }

        // Initialize  
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {  
            calculateTotalIncome();  
            updateVisualStructure();  
            selectIBO('you');  
        });  
    \</script\>  
\</body\>  
\</html\>

                            \<h5 class="text-sm font-medium mb-2"\>Select Months to Apply:\</h5\>  
                            \<div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 text-sm" id="monthCheckboxes"\>  
                                \<\!-- Month checkboxes populated by JavaScript \--\>  
                            \</div\>  
                        \</div\>  
                        \<div\>  
                            \<h5 class="text-sm font-medium mb-4"\>Income Projections\</h5\>  
                            \<div class="bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded"\>  
                                \<div class="text-sm text-gray-600"\>Selected Months: \<span id="selectedMonths"\>0\</span\>\</div\>  
                                \<div class="text-lg font-bold text-green-600" id="totalProjectedIncome"\>$0\</div\>  
                                \<div class="text-sm text-gray-600"\>Average Monthly Income: \<span id="averageMonthlyIncome"\>$0\</span\>\</div\>  
                            \</div\>  
                        \</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<button class="bg-blue-500 text-white px-6 py-2 rounded hover:bg-blue-600 transition-colors" onclick="applyToSelectedMonths()"\>  
                        \<i class="fas fa-copy mr-2"\>\</i\>Apply to Selected Months  
                    \</button\>  
                \</div\>  
            \</div\>  
              
            \<\!-- Visual Business Structures Section \--\>  
            \<div class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg"\>  
                \<div class="p-4 border-b border-gray-200"\>  
                    \<h3 class="text-lg font-semibold"\>Visual Business Structures by Month\</h3\>  
                    \<p class="text-sm text-gray-600 mt-1"\>Below are the actual visual business groups for each month with data\</p\>  
                \</div\>  
                \<div class="p-4"\>  
                    \<div id="visualStructuresContainer" class="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-3 gap-4"\>  
                        \<\!-- Visual structures will be populated by JavaScript \--\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
            \</div\>  
        \</div\>  
    \</div\>

    \<\!-- Analytics Tab \--\>  
    \<div id="analytics" class="tab-content hidden"\>  
        \<div class="container mx-auto px-4 py-6"\>  
            \<div class="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6"\>  
                \<\!-- Performance Analytics \--\>  
                \<div class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg"\>

                        \<canvas id="performanceChart" style="height: 300px;"\>\</canvas\>

                \<\!-- Income Trend \--\>  
                \<div class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg"\>  
                    \<div class="p-4 border-b border-gray-200"\>  
                        \<h3 class="text-lg font-semibold"\>Income Trend\</h3\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<div class="p-4"\>  
                        \<canvas id="incomeChart" style="height: 300px;"\>\</canvas\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>

                \<\!-- Team Performance \--\>  
                \<div class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg lg:col-span-2"\>  
                    \<div class="p-4 border-b border-gray-200"\>  
                        \<h3 class="text-lg font-semibold"\>Team Performance\</h3\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<div class="p-4"\>  
                        \<canvas id="teamChart" style="height: 300px;"\>\</canvas\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
            \</div\>  
        \</div\>  
    \</div\>

    \<\!-- All Incentives Tab \--\>  
    \<div id="incentives" class="tab-content hidden"\>  
        \<div class="container mx-auto px-4 py-6"\>  
            \<div class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg"\>  
                \<div class="p-4 border-b border-gray-200"\>  
                    \<h3 class="text-lg font-semibold"\>All Auto-Calculated Incentives & Bonuses\</h3\>  
                    \<p class="text-sm text-gray-600 mt-1"\>Based on your current business structure, here are all qualified incentives\</p\>  
                \</div\>  
                \<div class="p-4"\>  
                    \<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4" id="incentivesGrid"\>

    \<\!-- Reports Tab \--\>  
    \<div id="reports" class="tab-content hidden"\>  
        \<div class="container mx-auto px-4 py-6"\>  
            \<div class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg"\>  
                \<div class="p-4 border-b border-gray-200"\>  
                    \<h3 class="text-lg font-semibold"\>Comprehensive Business Reports\</h3\>  
                \</div\>  
                \<div class="p-4"\>  
                    \<div class="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6"\>  
                        \<\!-- Business Summary \--\>  
                        \<div class="border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-4"\>  
                            \<h4 class="font-semibold mb-4"\>Business Summary\</h4\>  
                            \<div class="space-y-2 text-sm" id="businessSummary"\>  
                                \<\!-- Summary populated by JavaScript \--\>

                        \</div\>

                        \<\!-- Income Breakdown \--\>  
                        \<div class="border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-4"\>

                                \<\!-- Breakdown populated by JavaScript \--\>
