    \<\!-- Official Amway Disclaimers \--\>  
    \<div class="disclaimer-box container mx-auto px-4"\>  
        \<h4 class="font-bold text-lg mb-4 text-orange-800"\>\<i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle mr-2"\>\</i\>Important Disclaimers\</h4\>  
          
        \<div class="space-y-4 text-sm text-orange-800"\>  
            \<div\>  
                \<strong\>Income Disclosure:\</strong\> For the calendar year 2023, the average income from Amway for all U.S. registered IBOs at the Founders Platinum level and below was $841 before expenses. See amway.com/income-disclosure for details and the most up-to-date information.  
            \</div\>  
              
            \<div\>  
                \<strong\>Results Vary:\</strong\> Earnings depend on many factors, including customer base, business experience, effort, dedication, and quality and performance of the downline sales team.  
            \</div\>  
              
            \<div\>  
                \<strong\>Baseline Requirements:\</strong\> IBOs must meet baseline requirements in order to be eligible to participate. Average of 150 Personal PV monthly, at least 60% from Verified Customer Sales, and adherence to Rules of Conduct are required.  
            \</div\>  
              
            \<div\>  
                \<strong\>Program Changes:\</strong\> All cash incentive payments for first time or recurring pin qualifications are part of our discretionary Core Plus discretionary incentives program and thus subject to change.  
            \</div\>  
              
            \<div\>  
                \<strong\>Achievement Statistics:\</strong\> The following percentages of IBOs achieved these incentive trips in 2023: New Platinum Conference 0.04459%; Achievers Invitational 0.49492%; Diamond Club 0.03177%; Diamond Select 0.01254%; NAGC 0.00920%.  
            \</div\>  
              
            \<div class="border-t pt-4"\>  
                \<strong\>Calculator Notice:\</strong\> This calculator provides estimates based on 2024 compensation plan data and should be used for planning purposes only. Actual results may vary based on individual circumstances, market conditions, and compliance with Amway policies.  
            \</div\>  
        \</div\>  
    \</div\>

    \<script\>  
        // Global Variables  
        let currentZoom \= 1;  
        let selectedNode \= 'you';  
        let businessData \= {  
            you: {  
                name: 'You',  
                pv: 150,  
                bv: 514.5,  
                vcsCompliant: true,  
                level: 3,  
                downlines: \[\]  
            }  
        };  
        let monthlyStructures \= {};  
        let currentMonth \= 'Aug2025';

        // Tab Navigation  
        document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(btn \=\> {  
            btn.addEventListener('click', function() {  
                const tabName \= this.dataset.tab;  
                showTab(tabName);  
                  
                // Update active tab styling  
                document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(b \=\> {  
                    b.classList.remove('border-indigo-500', 'text-indigo-600');  
                    b.classList.add('border-transparent', 'text-gray-500');  
                });  
                this.classList.add('border-indigo-500', 'text-indigo-600');  
                this.classList.remove('border-transparent', 'text-gray-500');  
            });  
        });

        function showTab(tabName) {  
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(tab \=\> {  
                tab.classList.add('hidden');  
            });  
            document.getElementById(tabName).classList.remove('hidden');  
              
            if (tabName \=== 'analytics') {  
                initializeCharts();  
            }  
            if (tabName \=== 'incentives') {  
                updateIncentivesDisplay();  
            }  
            if (tabName \=== 'reports') {  
                updateReportsDisplay();  
            }  
        }

        // Visual Builder Functions  
        function selectNode(nodeId) {  
            selectedNode \= nodeId;  
            updateMemberDetailsPanel(nodeId);  
              
            // Update visual selection  
            document.querySelectorAll('.ibs-node').forEach(node \=\> {  
                node.classList.remove('selected');  
            });  
            document.getElementById(nodeId \+ 'Node').classList.add('selected');  
        }

        function updateMemberDetailsPanel(nodeId) {  
            const data \= businessData\[nodeId\];  
            if (data) {  
                document.getElementById('memberName').value \= data.name;  
                document.getElementById('memberPV').value \= data.pv;  
                document.getElementById('memberBV').value \= data.bv;  
                document.getElementById('vcsCompliant').checked \= data.vcsCompliant;  
                document.getElementById('goalLevel').value \= data.level;  
            }  
        }

        function updateMemberData() {  
            const pv \= parseInt(document.getElementById('memberPV').value) || 0;  
            const bv \= pv \* 3.43;  
            document.getElementById('memberBV').value \= bv.toFixed(2);  
              
            // Update business data  
            businessData\[selectedNode\].pv \= pv;  
            businessData\[selectedNode\].bv \= bv;  
            businessData\[selectedNode\].name \= document.getElementById('memberName').value;  
            businessData\[selectedNode\].level \= parseInt(document.getElementById('goalLevel').value);  
              
            // Update visual display  
            updateNodeDisplay(selectedNode);  
            updateIncomeCalculations();  
        }

        function updateVCSCompliance() {  
            const compliant \= document.getElementById('vcsCompliant').checked;  
            businessData\[selectedNode\].vcsCompliant \= compliant;  
              
            if (\!compliant) {  
                // Prorate BV down by estimated compliance ratio  
                const originalBV \= businessData\[selectedNode\].pv \* 3.43;  
                businessData\[selectedNode\].bv \= originalBV \* 0.8; // Assume 80% compliance  
            } else {  
                businessData\[selectedNode\].bv \= businessData\[selectedNode\].pv \* 3.43;  
            }  
              
            document.getElementById('memberBV').value \= businessData\[selectedNode\].bv.toFixed(2);  
            updateNodeDisplay(selectedNode);  
            updateIncomeCalculations();  
        }

        function updateNodeDisplay(nodeId) {  
            const node \= document.getElementById(nodeId \+ 'Node');  
            const data \= businessData\[nodeId\];  
              
            if (node && data) {  
                node.querySelector('.font-bold').textContent \= data.name;  
                node.querySelector('\#' \+ nodeId \+ 'PV').textContent \= data.pv;  
                node.querySelector('\#' \+ nodeId \+ 'BV').textContent \= Math.round(data.bv);  
                node.querySelector('\#' \+ nodeId \+ 'Level').textContent \= data.level \+ '%';  
                  
                const vcsIcon \= node.querySelector('\#' \+ nodeId \+ 'VCS');  
                if (data.vcsCompliant) {  
                    vcsIcon.className \= 'fas fa-check-circle text-green-400 mr-1';  
                } else {  
                    vcsIcon.className \= 'fas fa-exclamation-triangle text-yellow-400 mr-1';  
                }  
            }  
        }

        function addDownline() {  
            const downlineId \= 'downline' \+ Date.now();  
            const parentData \= businessData\[selectedNode\];  
              
            // Create new downline data  
            businessData\[downlineId\] \= {  
                name: 'New IBO',  
                pv: 100,  
                bv: 343,  
                vcsCompliant: true,  
                level: 3,  
                downlines: \[\],  
                parent: selectedNode  
            };  
              
            // Add to parent's downlines  
            parentData.downlines.push(downlineId);  
              
            // Create visual node  
            createVisualNode(downlineId, parentData.downlines.length);  
            updateConnectionLines();  
            updateIncomeCalculations();  
        }

        function createVisualNode(nodeId, position) {  
            const data \= businessData\[nodeId\];  
            const node \= document.createElement('div');  
            node.id \= nodeId \+ 'Node';  
            node.className \= 'ibs-node';  
            node.style.top \= (200 \+ Math.floor(position / 5\) \* 150\) \+ 'px';  
            node.style.left \= (100 \+ (position % 5\) \* 140\) \+ 'px';  
            node.onclick \= () \=\> selectNode(nodeId);  
              
            node.innerHTML \= \`  
                \<div class="font-bold text-xs"\>${data.name}\</div\>  
                \<div id="${nodeId}Level" class="text-xs"\>${data.level}%\</div\>  
                \<div class="text-xs"\>PV: \<span id="${nodeId}PV"\>${data.pv}\</span\>\</div\>  
                \<div class="text-xs"\>BV: \<span id="${nodeId}BV"\>${Math.round(data.bv)}\</span\>\</div\>  
                \<div class="text-xs flex items-center mt-1"\>  
                    \<i id="${nodeId}VCS" class="fas fa-check-circle text-green-400 mr-1"\>\</i\>VCS  
                \</div\>  
            \`;  
              
            document.getElementById('orgChart').appendChild(node);  
        }

        function updateConnectionLines() {  
            const svg \= document.getElementById('connectionLines');  
            svg.innerHTML \= '';  
              
            // Draw lines from parent to children  
            Object.keys(businessData).forEach(nodeId \=\> {  
                const data \= businessData\[nodeId\];  
                data.downlines.forEach(childId \=\> {  
                    drawConnectionLine(svg, nodeId, childId);  
                });  
            });  
        }

        function drawConnectionLine(svg, parentId, childId) {  
            const parentNode \= document.getElementById(parentId \+ 'Node');  
            const childNode \= document.getElementById(childId \+ 'Node');  
              
            if (parentNode && childNode) {  
                const parentRect \= parentNode.getBoundingClientRect();  
                const childRect \= childNode.getBoundingClientRect();  
                const chartRect \= document.getElementById('orgChart').getBoundingClientRect();  
                  
                const x1 \= parentRect.left \+ parentRect.width/2 \- chartRect.left;  
                const y1 \= parentRect.top \+ parentRect.height \- chartRect.top;  
                const x2 \= childRect.left \+ childRect.width/2 \- chartRect.left;  
                const y2 \= childRect.top \- chartRect.top;  
                  
                const line \= document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'line');  
                line.setAttribute('x1', x1);  
                line.setAttribute('y1', y1);  
                line.setAttribute('x2', x2);  
                line.setAttribute('y2', y2);  
                line.setAttribute('class', 'connection-line');  
                  
                svg.appendChild(line);  
            }  
        }

        function updateIncomeCalculations() {  
            const data \= businessData\[selectedNode\];  
            const performanceBonus \= (data.bv \* data.level / 100);  
            const retailMargin \= data.pv \* 0.478; // Assuming 47.8% retail margin  
            const csi \= data.level \<= 9 ? data.bv \* (10 \- data.level) / 100 : 0;  
              
            const monthlyIncome \= performanceBonus \+ retailMargin \+ Math.min(csi, 75);  
              
            document.getElementById('monthlyIncome').textContent \= '$' \+ Math.round(monthlyIncome);  
            document.getElementById('performanceBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ Math.round(performanceBonus);  
            document.getElementById('leadershipBonus').textContent \= data.level \>= 25 ? '$1,544' : '$0';  
        }

        function toggleIncomeBreakdown(type) {  
            const breakdown \= document.getElementById(type \+ 'Breakdown');  
            breakdown.classList.toggle('show');  
        }

        // Zoom Functions  
        function zoomIn() {  
            currentZoom \= Math.min(currentZoom \* 1.2, 3);  
            applyZoom();  
        }

        function zoomOut() {  
            currentZoom \= Math.max(currentZoom / 1.2, 0.5);  
            applyZoom();  
        }

        function autoFit() {  
            currentZoom \= 1;  
            applyZoom();  
        }

        function applyZoom() {  
            const chart \= document.getElementById('orgChart');  
            chart.style.transform \= \`scale(${currentZoom})\`;  
        }

        function expandAll() {  
            // Expand all nodes logic  
        }

        function collapseAll() {  
            // Collapse all nodes logic  
        }

        // Multi-Month Functions  
        function pushToMultiMonth() {  
            const selectedMonth \= document.getElementById('monthSelect').value;  
            monthlyStructures\[selectedMonth\] \= JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(businessData));  
            updateTimelineDisplay();  
            updateVisualStructuresDisplay();  
        }

        function updateTimelineDisplay() {  
            const timeline \= document.getElementById('timelineContainer');  
            const months \= \['Aug2025', 'Sep2024', 'Oct2024', 'Nov2024', 'Dec2024', 'Jan2025', 'Feb2025', 'Mar2025', 'Apr2025'\];  
              
            timeline.innerHTML \= '';  
            months.forEach(month \=\> {  
                const hasData \= monthlyStructures\[month\];  
                const monthDiv \= document.createElement('div');  
                monthDiv.className \= \`timeline-month ${hasData ? 'selected' : ''}\`;  
                monthDiv.innerHTML \= \`  
                    \<h5 class="font-bold"\>${month}\</h5\>  
                    \<div class="text-sm"\>Total PV: ${hasData ? calculateTotalPV(monthlyStructures\[month\]) : 0}\</div\>  
                    \<div class="text-sm"\>Total BV: ${hasData ? calculateTotalBV(monthlyStructures\[month\]) : 0}\</div\>  
                    \<div class="text-sm"\>Members: ${hasData ? Object.keys(monthlyStructures\[month\]).length : 0}\</div\>  
                \`;  
                timeline.appendChild(monthDiv);  
            });  
        }

        function updateVisualStructuresDisplay() {  
            const container \= document.getElementById('visualStructuresContainer');  
            container.innerHTML \= '';  
              
            Object.keys(monthlyStructures).forEach(month \=\> {  
                const structure \= monthlyStructures\[month\];  
                const structureDiv \= document.createElement('div');  
                structureDiv.className \= 'visual-structure-display';  
                structureDiv.innerHTML \= \`  
                    \<h4 class="font-bold mb-4"\>${month}\</h4\>  
                    \<div class="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-2"\>Total PV: ${calculateTotalPV(structure)}\</div\>  
                    \<div class="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-4"\>Monthly Income: $${calculateMonthlyIncome(structure)}\</div\>  
                    \<div class="mini-org-chart"\>  
                        ${generateMiniChart(structure)}  
                    \</div\>  
                \`;  
                container.appendChild(structureDiv);  
            });  
        }

        function calculateTotalPV(structure) {  
            return Object.values(structure).reduce((total, member) \=\> total \+ member.pv, 0);  
        }

        function calculateTotalBV(structure) {  
            return Object.values(structure).reduce((total, member) \=\> total \+ member.bv, 0);  
        }

        function calculateMonthlyIncome(structure) {  
            return Object.values(structure).reduce((total, member) \=\> {  
                const performanceBonus \= member.bv \* member.level / 100;  
                return total \+ performanceBonus;  
            }, 0);  
        }

        function generateMiniChart(structure) {  
            // Generate a simplified visual representation  
            return Object.keys(structure).map(memberId \=\> {  
                const member \= structure\[memberId\];  
                return \`\<div class="inline-block bg-blue-500 text-white text-xs p-2 m-1 rounded"\>${member.name}\<br\>PV:${member.pv}\</div\>\`;  
            }).join('');  
        }

        // Incentive Calculations  
        function updateIncentivesDisplay() {  
            const grid \= document.getElementById('incentivesGrid');  
            const incentives \= calculateAllIncentives();  
              
            grid.innerHTML \= '';  
            incentives.forEach(incentive \=\> {  
                const card \= document.createElement('div');  
                card.className \= \`border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-4 ${incentive.qualified ? 'bg-green-50 border-green-200' : 'bg-gray-50'}\`;  
                card.innerHTML \= \`  
                    \<h4 class="font-bold text-lg ${incentive.qualified ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-gray-500'}"\>${incentive.name}\</h4\>  
                    \<div class="text-2xl font-bold mt-2 ${incentive.qualified ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-gray-400'}"\>$${incentive.amount}\</div\>  
                    \<div class="text-sm mt-2 ${incentive.qualified ? 'text-green-700' : 'text-gray-600'}"\>${incentive.description}\</div\>  
                    \<div class="mt-2"\>  
                        \<span class="px-2 py-1 text-xs rounded ${incentive.qualified ? 'bg-green-200 text-green-800' : 'bg-gray-200 text-gray-600'}"\>  
                            ${incentive.qualified ? 'QUALIFIED' : 'NOT QUALIFIED'}  
                        \</span\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \`;  
                grid.appendChild(card);  
            });  
        }

        function calculateAllIncentives() {  
            const totalPV \= calculateTotalPV(businessData);  
            const totalBV \= calculateTotalBV(businessData);  
            const memberCount \= Object.keys(businessData).length;  
              
            return \[  
                {  
                    name: 'Strong Start Incentive (SSI)',  
                    amount: totalPV \>= 150 ? 100 : 0,  
                    qualified: totalPV \>= 150,  
                    description: 'New IBOs: $100 after 3 months, up to $1,000 total'  
                },  
                {  
                    name: 'Bronze Foundation Incentive (BFI)',  
                    amount: totalPV \>= 150 ? 300 : 0,  
                    qualified: totalPV \>= 150,  
                    description: '30% multiplier \+ milestone bonuses up to $1,000'  
                },  
                {  
                    name: 'Ruby Bonus',  
                    amount: totalPV \>= 15000 ? totalBV \* 0.02 : 0,  
                    qualified: totalPV \>= 15000,  
                    description: '2% of Ruby BV for 15,000+ PV months'  
                },  
                {  
                    name: 'Platinum Two-Time Cash Incentive',  
                    amount: totalPV \>= 7500 ? 1500 : 0,  
                    qualified: totalPV \>= 7500,  
                    description: '$1,500 first-time, $2,500 consecutive year'  
                },  
                {  
                    name: 'Founders Platinum Incentive',  
                    amount: totalPV \>= 7500 ? 3500 : 0,  
                    qualified: totalPV \>= 7500 && memberCount \>= 12,  
                    description: '$3,500 first year, $7,500 second year'  
                },  
                {  
                    name: 'Leadership Bonus',  
                    amount: totalPV \>= 7500 ? 1544 : 0,  
                    qualified: totalPV \>= 7500,  
                    description: 'Monthly bonus for 25% Performance Bonus level'  
                },  
                {  
                    name: 'Emerald Bonus',  
                    amount: memberCount \>= 6 ? 5000 : 0,  
                    qualified: memberCount \>= 6,  
                    description: 'Three or more qualified groups at 25% level'  
                },  
                {  
                    name: 'Diamond Bonus',  
                    amount: memberCount \>= 10 ? 10000 : 0,  
                    qualified: memberCount \>= 10,  
                    description: 'Six or more qualified groups at 25% level'  
                }  
            \];  
        }

        // Analytics Functions  
        function initializeCharts() {  
            // Performance Chart  
            const performanceCtx \= document.getElementById('performanceChart').getContext('2d');  
            new Chart(performanceCtx, {  
                type: 'line',  
                data: {  
                    labels: \['Jan', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Apr', 'May', 'Jun'\],  
                    datasets: \[{  
                        label: 'PV Progress',  
                        data: \[150, 180, 220, 280, 350, 420\],  
                        borderColor: '\#4F46E5',  
                        backgroundColor: 'rgba(79, 70, 229, 0.1)',  
                        tension: 0.4  
                    }\]  
                },  
                options: {  
                    responsive: true,  
                    maintainAspectRatio: false  
                }  
            });

            // Income Chart  
            const incomeCtx \= document.getElementById('incomeChart').getContext('2d');  
            new Chart(incomeCtx, {  
                type: 'bar',  
                data: {  
                    labels: \['Jan', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Apr', 'May', 'Jun'\],  
                    datasets: \[{  
                        label: 'Monthly Income',  
                        data: \[232, 280, 340, 420, 525, 630\],  
                        backgroundColor: '\#10B981',  
                        borderColor: '\#059669',  
                        borderWidth: 1  
                    }\]  
                },  
                options: {  
                    responsive: true,  
                    maintainAspectRatio: false  
                }  
            });

            // Team Chart  
            const teamCtx \= document.getElementById('teamChart').getContext('2d');  
            new Chart(teamCtx, {  
                type: 'doughnut',  
                data: {  
                    labels: \['You', 'Frontline', 'Second Level', 'Third Level'\],  
                    datasets: \[{  
                        data: \[150, 400, 300, 200\],  
                        backgroundColor: \['\#4F46E5', '\#10B981', '\#F59E0B', '\#EF4444'\]  
                    }\]  
                },  
                options: {  
                    responsive: true,  
                    maintainAspectRatio: false  
                }  
            });  
        }

        function updateReportsDisplay() {  
            // Update business summary  
            const summary \= document.getElementById('businessSummary');  
            const totalPV \= calculateTotalPV(businessData);  
            const totalBV \= calculateTotalBV(businessData);  
            const memberCount \= Object.keys(businessData).length;  
              
            summary.innerHTML \= \`  
                \<div\>Total Organization PV: \<strong\>${totalPV}\</strong\>\</div\>  
                \<div\>Total Organization BV: \<strong\>${Math.round(totalBV)}\</strong\>\</div\>  
                \<div\>Total Team Members: \<strong\>${memberCount}\</strong\>\</div\>  
                \<div\>Performance Bonus Level: \<strong\>${businessData.you.level}%\</strong\>\</div\>  
                \<div\>VCS Compliance: \<strong\>${businessData.you.vcsCompliant ? 'Compliant' : 'Non-Compliant'}\</strong\>\</div\>  
            \`;

            // Update income breakdown  
            const breakdown \= document.getElementById('incomeBreakdownDetail');  
            const performanceBonus \= totalBV \* businessData.you.level / 100;  
            const retailMargin \= businessData.you.pv \* 0.478;  
            const csi \= businessData.you.level \<= 9 ? Math.min(businessData.you.bv \* (10 \- businessData.you.level) / 100, 75\) : 0;  
              
            breakdown.innerHTML \= \`  
                \<div\>Performance Bonus: \<strong\>$${Math.round(performanceBonus)}\</strong\>\</div\>  
                \<div\>Retail Margin: \<strong\>$${Math.round(retailMargin)}\</strong\>\</div\>  
                \<div\>Customer Sales Incentive: \<strong\>$${Math.round(csi)}\</strong\>\</div\>  
                \<div\>Leadership Bonus: \<strong\>$${businessData.you.level \>= 25 ? 1544 : 0}\</strong\>\</div\>  
                \<div class="border-t pt-2 mt-2"\>Total Monthly Income: \<strong\>$${Math.round(performanceBonus \+ retailMargin \+ csi)}\</strong\>\</div\>  
            \`;  
        }

        // Utility Functions  
        function saveCurrentMember() {  
            updateMemberData();  
            // Could add local storage save here  
        }

        function deleteIndividual() {  
            if (selectedNode \!== 'you' && confirm('Delete this individual? Their downline will move up to their upline.')) {  
                // Implementation for smart deletion  
            }  
        }

        function deleteGroup() {  
            if (selectedNode \!== 'you' && confirm('Delete this individual and their entire group?')) {  
                // Implementation for group deletion  
            }  
        }

        function switchPerspective() {  
            if (selectedNode \!== 'you') {  
                alert(\`Switching to ${businessData\[selectedNode\].name}'s perspective would show their income, bonuses, and team structure.\`);  
            }  
        }

        function applyToSelectedMonths() {  
            // Implementation for applying structure to multiple months  
        }

        // Initialize Month Checkboxes  
        function initializeMonthCheckboxes() {  
            const months \= \['Sep2024', 'Oct2024', 'Nov2024', 'Dec2024', 'Jan2025', 'Feb2025', 'Mar2025', 'Apr2025'\];  
            const container \= document.getElementById('monthCheckboxes');  
              
            months.forEach(month \=\> {  
                const label \= document.createElement('label');  
                label.className \= 'flex items-center';  
                label.innerHTML \= \`  
                    \<input type="checkbox" class="mr-1" value="${month}"\>  
                    \<span class="text-xs"\>${month}\</span\>  
                \`;  
                container.appendChild(label);  
            });  
        }

        // Initialize the application  
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {  
            initializeMonthCheckboxes();  
            updateIncomeCalculations();  
            updateTimelineDisplay();  
            updateVisualStructuresDisplay();  
        });  
    \</script\>  
\</body\>

                                \<span id="currentPinLevel" class="font-medium"\>New IBO\</span\>  
                            \</div\>

    \<script\>  
        // Global Variables  
        let currentSelectedNode \= null;  
        let businessData \= {  
            members: {  
                'root': {  
                    id: 'root',  
                    name: 'You',  
                    pv: 150,  
                    bv: 514.5,  
                    vcsCompliant: true,  
                    downline: \[\]  
                }  
            },  
            monthlyData: {},  
            zoomLevel: 1,  
            viewBox: { x: 0, y: 0, width: 800, height: 600 }  
        };

        // Tab Management  
        document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(btn \=\> {  
            btn.addEventListener('click', function() {  
                const targetTab \= this.dataset.tab;  
                  
                // Update active tab  
                document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(b \=\> b.classList.remove('active', 'text-blue-600', 'border-blue-600'));  
                document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(b \=\> b.classList.add('text-gray-500'));  
                this.classList.add('active', 'text-blue-600', 'border-b-2', 'border-blue-600');  
                this.classList.remove('text-gray-500');  
                  
                // Show target tab content  
                document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(content \=\> content.style.display \= 'none');  
                document.getElementById(targetTab).style.display \= 'block';  
                  
                // Initialize tab-specific content  
                if (targetTab \=== 'analytics') {  
                    initializeCharts();  
                } else if (targetTab \=== 'incentives') {  
                    calculateAllIncentives();  
                }  
            });  
        });

        // Member Details Form Handlers  
        document.getElementById('memberPV').addEventListener('input', function() {  
            const pv \= parseFloat(this.value) || 0;  
            const bv \= pv \* 3.43;  
            document.getElementById('memberBV').value \= bv.toFixed(2);  
            updateGoalLevel(pv);  
        });

        function updateGoalLevel(pv) {  
            const goalLevelSelect \= document.getElementById('goalLevel');  
            if (pv \>= 7500\) goalLevelSelect.value \= '25';  
            else if (pv \>= 6000\) goalLevelSelect.value \= '23';  
            else if (pv \>= 4000\) goalLevelSelect.value \= '21';  
            else if (pv \>= 2500\) goalLevelSelect.value \= '18';  
            else if (pv \>= 1500\) goalLevelSelect.value \= '15';  
            else if (pv \>= 1000\) goalLevelSelect.value \= '12';  
            else if (pv \>= 600\) goalLevelSelect.value \= '9';  
            else if (pv \>= 300\) goalLevelSelect.value \= '6';  
            else goalLevelSelect.value \= '3';  
        }

        // SVG Organization Chart Management  
        function initializeOrgChart() {  
            const svg \= document.getElementById('orgChart');  
            const rootNode \= document.getElementById('root-node');  
              
            rootNode.addEventListener('click', function() {  
                selectNode('root');  
            });  
              
            updateOrgChart();  
        }

        function selectNode(nodeId) {  
            currentSelectedNode \= nodeId;  
            const member \= businessData.members\[nodeId\];  
              
            // Update visual selection  
            document.querySelectorAll('.ibc-node').forEach(node \=\> {  
                node.classList.remove('selected');  
            });  
            document.getElementById(\`node-${nodeId}\`) && document.getElementById(\`node-${nodeId}\`).classList.add('selected');  
            document.getElementById('root-node').classList.remove('selected');  
            if (nodeId \=== 'root') document.getElementById('root-node').classList.add('selected');  
              
            // Populate member details form  
            document.getElementById('memberName').value \= member.name || '';  
            document.getElementById('memberPV').value \= member.pv || 0;  
            document.getElementById('memberBV').value \= member.bv || 0;  
            document.getElementById('vcsCompliance').checked \= member.vcsCompliant || false;  
            updateGoalLevel(member.pv || 0);  
        }

        function addDownlineMember() {  
            if (\!currentSelectedNode) return;  
              
            const newId \= 'member\_' \+ Date.now();  
            const newMember \= {  
                id: newId,  
                name: 'New IBO',  
                pv: 100,  
                bv: 343,  
                vcsCompliant: true,  
                downline: \[\]  
            };  
              
            businessData.members\[newId\] \= newMember;  
            businessData.members\[currentSelectedNode\].downline.push(newId);  
              
            updateOrgChart();  
            calculateAllIncome();  
        }

        function deleteMember() {  
            if (\!currentSelectedNode || currentSelectedNode \=== 'root') return;  
              
            // Move downline up one level  
            const member \= businessData.members\[currentSelectedNode\];  
            const parentId \= findParentNode(currentSelectedNode);  
              
            if (parentId && member.downline.length \> 0\) {  
                businessData.members\[parentId\].downline \= businessData.members\[parentId\].downline.concat(member.downline);  
            }  
              
            // Remove from parent's downline  
            if (parentId) {  
                businessData.members\[parentId\].downline \= businessData.members\[parentId\].downline.filter(id \=\> id \!== currentSelectedNode);  
            }  
              
            delete businessData.members\[currentSelectedNode\];  
            currentSelectedNode \= 'root';  
            updateOrgChart();  
            calculateAllIncome();  
        }

        function deleteGroup() {  
            if (\!currentSelectedNode || currentSelectedNode \=== 'root') return;  
              
            // Delete member and entire downline  
            function deleteRecursively(nodeId) {  
                const member \= businessData.members\[nodeId\];  
                if (member && member.downline) {  
                    member.downline.forEach(childId \=\> deleteRecursively(childId));  
                }  
                delete businessData.members\[nodeId\];  
            }  
              
            const parentId \= findParentNode(currentSelectedNode);  
            if (parentId) {  
                businessData.members\[parentId\].downline \= businessData.members\[parentId\].downline.filter(id \=\> id \!== currentSelectedNode);  
            }  
              
            deleteRecursively(currentSelectedNode);  
            currentSelectedNode \= 'root';  
            updateOrgChart();  
            calculateAllIncome();  
        }

        function findParentNode(nodeId) {  
            for (const \[memberId, member\] of Object.entries(businessData.members)) {  
                if (member.downline && member.downline.includes(nodeId)) {  
                    return memberId;  
                }  
            }  
            return null;  
        }

        function updateOrgChart() {  
            const svg \= document.getElementById('orgChart');  
              
            // Clear existing elements except root  
            const existingNodes \= svg.querySelectorAll('.ibc-node:not(\#root-node)');  
            const existingTexts \= svg.querySelectorAll('.node-text:not(\[x="400"\])');  
            const existingLines \= svg.querySelectorAll('.connection-line');  
              
            existingNodes.forEach(el \=\> el.remove());  
            existingTexts.forEach(el \=\> el.remove());  
            existingLines.forEach(el \=\> el.remove());  
              
            // Draw organization recursively  
            drawOrganization('root', 400, 100, 1);  
        }

        function drawOrganization(nodeId, x, y, level) {  
            const member \= businessData.members\[nodeId\];  
            if (\!member || \!member.downline || member.downline.length \=== 0\) return;  
              
            const downlineCount \= member.downline.length;  
            const spacing \= Math.max(120, 800 / (downlineCount \+ 1));  
            const startX \= 400 \- (spacing \* (downlineCount \- 1)) / 2;  
            const childY \= y \+ 120;  
              
            member.downline.forEach((childId, index) \=\> {  
                const childX \= startX \+ (spacing \* index);  
                const child \= businessData.members\[childId\];  
                  
                if (child) {  
                    // Draw connection line  
                    const line \= document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "line");  
                    line.setAttribute('class', 'connection-line');  
                    line.setAttribute('x1', x);  
                    line.setAttribute('y1', y \+ 40);  
                    line.setAttribute('x2', childX);  
                    line.setAttribute('y2', childY \- 40);  
                    svg.appendChild(line);  
                      
                    // Draw child node  
                    const circle \= document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "circle");  
                    circle.setAttribute('class', 'ibc-node');  
                    circle.setAttribute('id', \`node-${childId}\`);  
                    circle.setAttribute('cx', childX);  
                    circle.setAttribute('cy', childY);  
                    circle.setAttribute('r', 35);  
                    circle.setAttribute('filter', 'url(\#shadow)');  
                    circle.addEventListener('click', () \=\> selectNode(childId));  
                    svg.appendChild(circle);  
                      
                    // VCS compliance indicator  
                    const vcsIndicator \= document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "circle");  
                    vcsIndicator.setAttribute('cx', childX \+ 25);  
                    vcsIndicator.setAttribute('cy', childY \- 25);  
                    vcsIndicator.setAttribute('r', 6);  
                    vcsIndicator.setAttribute('fill', child.vcsCompliant ? '\#10b981' : '\#ef4444');  
                    svg.appendChild(vcsIndicator);  
                      
                    // Add text labels  
                    const nameText \= document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "text");  
                    nameText.setAttribute('class', 'node-text');  
                    nameText.setAttribute('x', childX);  
                    nameText.setAttribute('y', childY \- 10);  
                    nameText.textContent \= child.name || 'New IBO';  
                    svg.appendChild(nameText);  
                      
                    const pvText \= document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "text");  
                    pvText.setAttribute('class', 'node-text');  
                    pvText.setAttribute('x', childX);  
                    pvText.setAttribute('y', childY \+ 5);  
                    pvText.setAttribute('style', 'font-size: 10px;');  
                    pvText.textContent \= \`${child.pv} PV\`;  
                    svg.appendChild(pvText);  
                      
                    const bvText \= document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "text");  
                    bvText.setAttribute('class', 'node-text');  
                    bvText.setAttribute('x', childX);  
                    bvText.setAttribute('y', childY \+ 18);  
                    bvText.setAttribute('style', 'font-size: 10px;');  
                    bvText.textContent \= \`${child.bv.toFixed(0)} BV\`;  
                    svg.appendChild(bvText);  
                      
                    // Recursively draw children  
                    drawOrganization(childId, childX, childY, level \+ 1);  
                }  
            });  
        }

        // Income Calculations  
        function calculateAllIncome() {  
            const totalPV \= calculateTotalPV();  
            const totalBV \= calculateTotalBV();  
            const performanceBonus \= calculatePerformanceBonus(totalPV, totalBV);  
            const leadershipBonus \= calculateLeadershipBonus();  
            const monthlyIncome \= performanceBonus \+ leadershipBonus;  
              
            document.getElementById('monthlyIncome').textContent \= '$' \+ monthlyIncome.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('performanceBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ performanceBonus.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('leadershipBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ leadershipBonus.toFixed(0);  
        }

        function calculateTotalPV() {  
            let total \= 0;  
            for (const member of Object.values(businessData.members)) {  
                total \+= member.pv || 0;  
            }  
            return total;  
        }

        function calculateTotalBV() {  
            let total \= 0;  
            for (const member of Object.values(businessData.members)) {  
                const effectiveBV \= member.vcsCompliant ? member.bv : (member.bv \* 0.7); // Prorate if not VCS compliant  
                total \+= effectiveBV || 0;  
            }  
            return total;  
        }

        function calculatePerformanceBonus(pv, bv) {  
            let percentage \= 0;  
            if (pv \>= 7500\) percentage \= 0.25;  
            else if (pv \>= 6000\) percentage \= 0.23;  
            else if (pv \>= 4000\) percentage \= 0.21;  
            else if (pv \>= 2500\) percentage \= 0.18;  
            else if (pv \>= 1500\) percentage \= 0.15;  
            else if (pv \>= 1000\) percentage \= 0.12;  
            else if (pv \>= 600\) percentage \= 0.09;  
            else if (pv \>= 300\) percentage \= 0.06;  
            else if (pv \>= 100\) percentage \= 0.03;  
              
            return bv \* percentage;  
        }

        function calculateLeadershipBonus() {  
            // Simplified leadership bonus calculation  
            const totalPV \= calculateTotalPV();  
            if (totalPV \>= 7500\) {  
                return Math.max(1543.50, totalPV \* 0.04); // Minimum guaranteed or 4% of total  
            }  
            return 0;  
        }

        function calculateAllIncentives() {  
            const totalPV \= calculateTotalPV();  
            const totalBV \= calculateTotalBV();  
            const rootMember \= businessData.members\['root'\];  
              
            // Core Plan Calculations  
            const retailMargin \= (rootMember.pv || 0\) \* 0.1 \* 2.84; // 10% margin on retail sales  
            const performanceBonus \= calculatePerformanceBonus(totalPV, totalBV);  
            const differentialBonus \= calculateDifferentialBonus();  
            const csiBonus \= Math.min(75, calculateCSIBonus()); // Max $75/month  
            const rubyBonus \= totalPV \>= 15000 ? totalBV \* 0.02 : 0;  
            const leadershipBonus \= calculateLeadershipBonus();  
            const depthBonus \= calculateDepthBonus();  
              
            // New IBO Incentives  
            const ssiBonus \= calculateSSIBonus();  
            const bfiBonus \= calculateBFIBonus();  
            const bfiMultiplier \= calculateBFIMultiplier();  
            const bbiBonus \= calculateBBIBonus();  
            const bbiMultiplier \= calculateBBIMultiplier();  
              
            // Leadership Incentives  
            const pggiBonus \= calculatePGGIBonus();  
            const performancePlus \= calculatePerformancePlusElite();  
            const fgiBonus \= calculateFGIBonus();  
            const emeraldBonus \= calculateEmeraldBonus();  
            const diamondBonus \= calculateDiamondBonus();  
            const diamondPlusBonus \= calculateDiamondPlusBonus();  
              
            // Two-Time Cash Incentives  
            const platinumTTCI \= calculatePlatinumTTCI();  
            const foundersPlatinumTTCI \= calculateFoundersPlatinumTTCI();  
            const emeraldTTCI \= calculateEmeraldTTCI();  
            const diamondTTCI \= calculateDiamondTTCI();  
            const foundersDiamondTTCI \= calculateFoundersDiamondTTCI();  
              
            // High-Level Awards  
            const faaBonus \= calculateFAABonus();  
            const superLegsBonus \= calculateSuperLegsBonus();  
            const garBonus \= calculateGARBonus();  
            const emeraldProfitSharing \= calculateEmeraldProfitSharing();  
              
            // Update UI  
            document.getElementById('retailMargin').textContent \= '$' \+ retailMargin.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('performanceBonusInc').textContent \= '$' \+ performanceBonus.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('differentialBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ differentialBonus.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('csiBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ csiBonus.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('rubyBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ rubyBonus.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('leadershipBonusInc').textContent \= '$' \+ leadershipBonus.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('depthBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ depthBonus.toFixed(0);  
              
            document.getElementById('ssiBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ ssiBonus.toFixed(0) \+ ' / $1,000';  
            document.getElementById('bfiBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ bfiBonus.toFixed(0) \+ ' / $1,000';  
            document.getElementById('bfiMultiplier').textContent \= '$' \+ bfiMultiplier.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('bbiBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ bbiBonus.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('bbiMultiplier').textContent \= '$' \+ bbiMultiplier.toFixed(0);  
              
            document.getElementById('pggiBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ pggiBonus.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('performancePlus').textContent \= '$' \+ performancePlus.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('fgiBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ fgiBonus.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('emeraldBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ emeraldBonus.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('diamondBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ diamondBonus.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('diamondPlusBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ diamondPlusBonus.toFixed(0);  
              
            document.getElementById('platinumTTCI').textContent \= '$' \+ platinumTTCI.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('foundersPlatinumTTCI').textContent \= '$' \+ foundersPlatinumTTCI.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('emeraldTTCI').textContent \= '$' \+ emeraldTTCI.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('diamondTTCI').textContent \= '$' \+ diamondTTCI.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('foundersDiamondTTCI').textContent \= '$' \+ foundersDiamondTTCI.toFixed(0);  
              
            document.getElementById('faaBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ faaBonus.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('superLegsBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ superLegsBonus.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('garBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ garBonus.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('emeraldProfitSharing').textContent \= '$' \+ emeraldProfitSharing.toFixed(0);  
              
            // Update event qualifications  
            updateEventQualifications(totalPV);  
              
            // Calculate totals  
            const totalCoreIncome \= retailMargin \+ performanceBonus \+ differentialBonus \+ csiBonus \+ rubyBonus \+ leadershipBonus \+ depthBonus;  
            const totalCorePlusIncome \= ssiBonus \+ bfiBonus \+ bfiMultiplier \+ bbiBonus \+ bbiMultiplier \+ pggiBonus \+ performancePlus \+ fgiBonus \+ emeraldBonus \+ diamondBonus \+ diamondPlusBonus \+ platinumTTCI \+ foundersPlatinumTTCI \+ emeraldTTCI \+ diamondTTCI \+ foundersDiamondTTCI \+ faaBonus \+ superLegsBonus \+ garBonus \+ emeraldProfitSharing;  
            const totalMonthlyIncome \= totalCoreIncome \+ totalCorePlusIncome;  
              
            document.getElementById('totalCoreIncome').textContent \= '$' \+ totalCoreIncome.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('totalCorePlusIncome').textContent \= '$' \+ totalCorePlusIncome.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('totalMonthlyIncome').textContent \= '$' \+ totalMonthlyIncome.toFixed(0);  
        }

        // Individual incentive calculation functions  
        function calculateDifferentialBonus() {  
            // Simplified differential bonus calculation  
            return 0; // Would need complex downline comparison  
        }

        function calculateCSIBonus() {  
            const rootMember \= businessData.members\['root'\];  
            const performanceLevel \= getPerformanceLevel(calculateTotalPV());  
            if (performanceLevel \<= 9 && rootMember.vcsCompliant) {  
                const vcsBonus \= (10 \- performanceLevel) / 100;  
                return Math.min(75, rootMember.bv \* vcsBonus);  
            }  
            return 0;  
        }

        function calculateDepthBonus() {  
            const legs \= businessData.members\['root'\].downline || \[\];  
            const qualifiedLegs \= legs.filter(legId \=\> {  
                const member \= businessData.members\[legId\];  
                return member && getPerformanceLevel(calculateMemberTotalPV(legId)) \>= 25;  
            });  
              
            if (qualifiedLegs.length \>= 3\) {  
                let depthBonus \= 0;  
                qualifiedLegs.forEach(legId \=\> {  
                    const legBV \= calculateMemberTotalBV(legId);  
                    depthBonus \+= legBV \* 0.01; // 1% depth bonus  
                });  
                return depthBonus;  
            }  
            return 0;  
        }

        function calculateSSIBonus() {  
            // Would need to track months and qualification \- simplified  
            return 0;  
        }

            // Would need to track months and qualification \- simplified  
            return 0;  
        }

            // 30% multiplier on performance bonus if qualified  
            return 0;  
        }

        function calculateBBIBonus() {  
            // 40% multiplier for Bronze Builder  
            return 0;  
        }

        function calculateBBIMultiplier() {  
            return 0;  
        }

        function calculatePGGIBonus() {  
            // Personal Group Growth Incentive  
            return 0;  
        }

        function calculatePerformancePlusElite() {  
            const totalPV \= calculateTotalPV();  
            if (totalPV \>= 12500\) {  
                return calculateTotalBV() \* 0.04; // 4% for Performance Elite  
            } else if (totalPV \>= 10000\) {  
                return calculateTotalBV() \* 0.02; // 2% for Performance Plus  
            }  
            return 0;  
        }

        function calculateFGIBonus() {  
            // Frontline Growth Incentive  
            return 0;  
        }

        function calculateEmeraldBonus() {  
            const legs \= businessData.members\['root'\].downline || \[\];  
            const qualifiedLegs \= legs.filter(legId \=\> {  
                const member \= businessData.members\[legId\];  
                return member && getPerformanceLevel(calculateMemberTotalPV(legId)) \>= 25;  
            });  
              
            if (qualifiedLegs.length \>= 3\) {  
                // Simplified Emerald bonus calculation  
                return 500; // Base amount  
            }  
            return 0;  
        }

        function calculateDiamondBonus() {  
            const legs \= businessData.members\['root'\].downline || \[\];  
            const qualifiedLegs \= legs.filter(legId \=\> {  
                const member \= businessData.members\[legId\];  
                return member && getPerformanceLevel(calculateMemberTotalPV(legId)) \>= 25;  
            });  
              
            if (qualifiedLegs.length \>= 6\) {  
                // Simplified Diamond bonus calculation  
                return 2000; // Base amount  
            }  
            return 0;  
        }

        function calculateDiamondPlusBonus() {  
            const legs \= businessData.members\['root'\].downline || \[\];  
            const qualifiedLegs \= legs.filter(legId \=\> {  
                const member \= businessData.members\[legId\];  
                return member && getPerformanceLevel(calculateMemberTotalPV(legId)) \>= 25;  
            });  
              
            if (qualifiedLegs.length \>= 7\) {  
                // Diamond Plus bonus based on number of legs  
                const bonusPerLeg \= Math.min(13200, 4200 \+ (qualifiedLegs.length \- 7\) \* 1000);  
                return bonusPerLeg \* qualifiedLegs.length;  
            }  
            return 0;  
        }

        function calculatePlatinumTTCI() {  
            const totalPV \= calculateTotalPV();  
            if (totalPV \>= 7500\) {  
                return 1500; // First-time Platinum bonus  
            }  
            return 0;  
        }

        function updateEventQualifications(totalPV) {  
            const npc \= totalPV \>= 7500 ? 'Qualified' : 'Not Qualified';  
            const achievers \= totalPV \>= 7500 ? 'Qualified' : 'Not Qualified'; // Simplified  
            const diamondClub \= calculateDiamondBonus() \> 0 ? 'Qualified' : 'Not Qualified';  
            const growthCouncil \= calculateGARBonus() \> 0 ? 'Qualified' : 'Not Qualified';  
              
            document.getElementById('npcQual').textContent \= npc;  
            document.getElementById('achieversQual').textContent \= achievers;  
            document.getElementById('diamondClubQual').textContent \= diamondClub;  
            document.getElementById('growthCouncilQual').textContent \= growthCouncil;  
              
            // Update colors  
            document.getElementById('npcQual').className \= npc \=== 'Qualified' ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-red-600';  
            document.getElementById('achieversQual').className \= achievers \=== 'Qualified' ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-red-600';  
            document.getElementById('diamondClubQual').className \= diamondClub \=== 'Qualified' ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-red-600';  
            document.getElementById('growthCouncilQual').className \= growthCouncil \=== 'Qualified' ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-red-600';  
        }

        // Helper functions  
        function getPerformanceLevel(pv) {  
            if (pv \>= 7500\) return 25;  
            else if (pv \>= 6000\) return 23;  
            else if (pv \>= 4000\) return 21;  
            else if (pv \>= 2500\) return 18;  
            else if (pv \>= 1500\) return 15;  
            else if (pv \>= 1000\) return 12;  
            else if (pv \>= 600\) return 9;  
            else if (pv \>= 300\) return 6;  
            else return 3;  
        }

        function calculateMemberTotalPV(memberId) {  
            let total \= 0;  
            function addPVRecursively(nodeId) {  
                const member \= businessData.members\[nodeId\];  
                if (member) {  
                    total \+= member.pv || 0;  
                    if (member.downline) {  
                        member.downline.forEach(childId \=\> addPVRecursively(childId));  
                    }  
                }  
            }  
            addPVRecursively(memberId);  
            return total;  
        }

        function calculateMemberTotalBV(memberId) {  
            let total \= 0;  
            function addBVRecursively(nodeId) {  
                const member \= businessData.members\[nodeId\];  
                if (member) {  
                    const effectiveBV \= member.vcsCompliant ? member.bv : (member.bv \* 0.7);  
                    total \+= effectiveBV || 0;  
                    if (member.downline) {  
                        member.downline.forEach(childId \=\> addBVRecursively(childId));  
                    }  
                }  
            }  
            addBVRecursively(memberId);  
            return total;  
        }

        // UI Interaction Functions  
        function toggleBreakdown(type) {  
            const breakdown \= document.getElementById(type \+ 'Breakdown');  
            const isVisible \= breakdown.style.display \!== 'none';  
              
            // Hide all breakdowns first  
            document.querySelectorAll('.income-breakdown').forEach(el \=\> el.style.display \= 'none');  
              
            if (\!isVisible) {  
                breakdown.style.display \= 'block';  
                generateBreakdownContent(type);  
            }  
        }

        function generateBreakdownContent(type) {  
            const totalPV \= calculateTotalPV();  
            const totalBV \= calculateTotalBV();  
            let content \= '';  
              
            if (type \=== 'monthly') {  
                const performanceBonus \= calculatePerformanceBonus(totalPV, totalBV);  
                const leadershipBonus \= calculateLeadershipBonus();  
                const total \= performanceBonus \+ leadershipBonus;  
                  
                content \= \`  
                    \<div\>\<strong\>Performance Bonus:\</strong\> $${performanceBonus.toFixed(2)}\</div\>  
                    \<div class="text-gray-600 text-xs ml-4"\>${totalPV} PV √ó ${getPerformanceLevel(totalPV)}% \= $${performanceBonus.toFixed(2)}\</div\>  
                    \<div\>\<strong\>Leadership Bonus:\</strong\> $${leadershipBonus.toFixed(2)}\</div\>  
                    \<div class="text-gray-600 text-xs ml-4"\>Minimum guaranteed for 25% level\</div\>  
                    \<div class="border-t pt-2 mt-2"\>\<strong\>Total Monthly Income:\</strong\> $${total.toFixed(2)}\</div\>  
                \`;  
            } else if (type \=== 'performance') {  
                const bonus \= calculatePerformanceBonus(totalPV, totalBV);  
                const percentage \= getPerformanceLevel(totalPV);  
                  
                content \= \`  
                    \<div\>\<strong\>Total PV:\</strong\> ${totalPV}\</div\>  
                    \<div\>\<strong\>Total BV:\</strong\> ${totalBV.toFixed(2)}\</div\>  
                    \<div\>\<strong\>Performance Level:\</strong\> ${percentage}%\</div\>  
                    \<div class="text-gray-600 text-xs"\>VCS adjustments applied to non-compliant members\</div\>  
                    \<div class="border-t pt-2 mt-2"\>\<strong\>Performance Bonus:\</strong\> $${bonus.toFixed(2)}\</div\>  
                \`;  
            } else if (type \=== 'leadership') {  
                const bonus \= calculateLeadershipBonus();  
                  
                content \= \`  
                    \<div\>\<strong\>Qualification:\</strong\> ${totalPV \>= 7500 ? 'Qualified (25% level)' : 'Not Qualified'}\</div\>  
                    \<div\>\<strong\>Group Volume:\</strong\> ${totalBV.toFixed(2)} BV\</div\>  
                    \<div\>\<strong\>Minimum Guaranteed:\</strong\> $1,543.50\</div\>  
                    \<div\>\<strong\>Volume Bonus (4%):\</strong\> $${(totalPV \* 0.04).toFixed(2)}\</div\>  
                    \<div class="border-t pt-2 mt-2"\>\<strong\>Leadership Bonus:\</strong\> $${bonus.toFixed(2)}\</div\>  
                \`;  
            }  
              
            document.getElementById(type \+ 'BreakdownContent').innerHTML \= content;  
        }

        function toggleIncentiveBreakdown() {  
            const calculations \= document.getElementById('incentiveCalculations');  
            const isVisible \= calculations.style.display \!== 'none';  
            calculations.style.display \= isVisible ? 'none' : 'block';  
              
            if (\!isVisible) {  
                generateIncentiveCalculations();  
            }  
        }

        function generateIncentiveCalculations() {  
            const content \= \`  
                \<div class="space-y-4"\>  
                    \<div class="bg-white p-4 rounded-lg"\>  
                        \<h5 class="font-bold text-gray-800 mb-2"\>Performance Bonus Calculation\</h5\>  
                        \<p class="text-xs text-gray-600"\>Total PV: ${calculateTotalPV()} ‚Üí Performance Level: ${getPerformanceLevel(calculateTotalPV())}%\</p\>  
                        \<p class="text-xs text-gray-600"\>Total BV: ${calculateTotalBV().toFixed(2)} √ó ${getPerformanceLevel(calculateTotalPV())}% \= $${calculatePerformanceBonus(calculateTotalPV(), calculateTotalBV()).toFixed(2)}\</p\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<div class="bg-white p-4 rounded-lg"\>  
                        \<h5 class="font-bold text-gray-800 mb-2"\>VCS Compliance Impact\</h5\>  
                        \<p class="text-xs text-gray-600"\>Non-VCS compliant members have BV reduced by 30% (70% customer sales requirement)\</p\>  
                        \<p class="text-xs text-gray-600"\>This affects all upline bonus calculations\</p\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<div class="bg-white p-4 rounded-lg"\>  
                        \<h5 class="font-bold text-gray-800 mb-2"\>Qualification Status\</h5\>  
                        \<p class="text-xs text-gray-600"\>Current Pin Level: ${getCurrentPinLevel()}\</p\>  
                        \<p class="text-xs text-gray-600"\>Next Goal: ${getNextPinGoal()}\</p\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
            \`;  
            document.getElementById('incentiveCalculationsContent').innerHTML \= content;  
        }

        function getCurrentPinLevel() {  
            const totalPV \= calculateTotalPV();  
            const legs \= businessData.members\['root'\].downline || \[\];  
            const qualifiedLegs \= legs.filter(legId \=\> {  
                const member \= businessData.members\[legId\];  
                return member && getPerformanceLevel(calculateMemberTotalPV(legId)) \>= 25;  
            });  
              
            if (qualifiedLegs.length \>= 6\) return 'Diamond';  
            else if (qualifiedLegs.length \>= 3\) return 'Emerald';  
            else if (totalPV \>= 7500\) return 'Silver Producer';  
            else return 'New IBO';  
        }

        function getNextPinGoal() {  
            const currentPin \= getCurrentPinLevel();  
            if (currentPin \=== 'New IBO') return 'Silver Producer (7,500 PV)';  
            else if (currentPin \=== 'Silver Producer') return 'Emerald (3 legs at 25%)';  
            else if (currentPin \=== 'Emerald') return 'Diamond (6 legs at 25%)';  
            else return 'Higher Diamond Levels';  
        }

        // Charts Initialization  
        function initializeCharts() {  
            initPerformanceChart();  
            initIncomeChart();  
            initTeamChart();  
            initGoalProgress();  
        }

        function initPerformanceChart() {  
            const ctx \= document.getElementById('performanceChart').getContext('2d');  
            new Chart(ctx, {  
                type: 'line',  
                data: {  
                    labels: \['Sep', 'Oct', 'Nov', 'Dec', 'Jan', 'Feb'\],  
                    datasets: \[{  
                        label: 'Monthly Income',  
                        data: \[200, 350, 500, 750, 1200, 1800\],  
                        borderColor: '\#3b82f6',  
                        backgroundColor: 'rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.1)',  
                        fill: true,  
                        tension: 0.4  
                    }\]  
                },  
                options: {  
                    responsive: true,  
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,  
                    plugins: {  
                        legend: { position: 'top' }  
                    },  
                    scales: {  
                        y: { beginAtZero: true }  
                    }  
                }  
            });  
        }

        function initIncomeChart() {  
            const ctx \= document.getElementById('incomeChart').getContext('2d');  
            new Chart(ctx, {  
                type: 'doughnut',  
                data: {  
                    labels: \['Performance Bonus', 'Leadership Bonus', 'Retail Margin', 'Other Incentives'\],  
                    datasets: \[{  
                        data: \[60, 25, 10, 5\],  
                        backgroundColor: \['\#3b82f6', '\#8b5cf6', '\#10b981', '\#f59e0b'\]  
                    }\]  
                },  
                options: {  
                    responsive: true,  
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,  
                    plugins: {  
                        legend: { position: 'bottom' }  
                    }  
                }  
            });  
        }

        function initTeamChart() {  
            const ctx \= document.getElementById('teamChart').getContext('2d');  
            new Chart(ctx, {  
                type: 'bar',  
                data: {  
                    labels: \['Level 1', 'Level 2', 'Level 3', 'Level 4'\],  
                    datasets: \[{  
                        label: 'Team Members',  
                        data: \[3, 9, 15, 8\],  
                        backgroundColor: '\#3b82f6'  
                    }, {  
                        label: 'VCS Compliant',  
                        data: \[3, 7, 12, 6\],  
                        backgroundColor: '\#10b981'  
                    }\]  
                },  
                options: {  
                    responsive: true,  
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,  
                    plugins: {  
                        legend: { position: 'top' }  
                    },  
                    scales: {  
                        y: { beginAtZero: true }  
                    }  
                }  
            });  
        }

        function initGoalProgress() {  
            const goalProgress \= document.getElementById('goalProgress');  
            goalProgress.innerHTML \= \`  
                \<div class="bg-gray-100 rounded-lg p-4"\>  
                    \<div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-2"\>  
                        \<span class="font-medium"\>Silver Producer Goal\</span\>  
                        \<span class="text-sm text-gray-600"\>${calculateTotalPV()} / 7,500 PV\</span\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<div class="w-full bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-2"\>  
                        \<div class="bg-blue-600 h-2 rounded-full" style="width: ${Math.min(100, (calculateTotalPV() / 7500\) \* 100)}%"\>\</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
                \<div class="bg-gray-100 rounded-lg p-4"\>  
                    \<div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-2"\>  
                        \<span class="font-medium"\>Monthly Income Goal\</span\>  
                        \<span class="text-sm text-gray-600"\>$${parseFloat(document.getElementById('monthlyIncome').textContent.replace('$', '') || 0).toFixed(0)} / $2,000\</span\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<div class="w-full bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-2"\>  
                        \<div class="bg-green-600 h-2 rounded-full" style="width: ${Math.min(100, (parseFloat(document.getElementById('monthlyIncome').textContent.replace('$', '') || 0\) / 2000\) \* 100)}%"\>\</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
            \`;  
        }

        // Zoom Controls  
        document.getElementById('zoomIn').addEventListener('click', function() {  
            businessData.zoomLevel \= Math.min(3, businessData.zoomLevel \* 1.2);  
            applyZoom();  
        });

        document.getElementById('zoomOut').addEventListener('click', function() {  
            businessData.zoomLevel \= Math.max(0.5, businessData.zoomLevel \* 0.8);  
            applyZoom();  
        });

        document.getElementById('autoZoom').addEventListener('click', function() {  
            businessData.zoomLevel \= 1;  
            applyZoom();  
        });

        function applyZoom() {  
            const svg \= document.getElementById('orgChart');  
            const centerX \= 400;  
            const centerY \= 300;  
            const newWidth \= 800 / businessData.zoomLevel;  
            const newHeight \= 600 / businessData.zoomLevel;  
            const newX \= centerX \- newWidth / 2;  
            const newY \= centerY \- newHeight / 2;  
              
            svg.setAttribute('viewBox', \`${newX} ${newY} ${newWidth} ${newHeight}\`);  
        }

        // Event Listeners  
        document.getElementById('saveMember').addEventListener('click', function() {  
            if (\!currentSelectedNode) return;  
              
            const member \= businessData.members\[currentSelectedNode\];  
            member.name \= document.getElementById('memberName').value || member.name;  
            member.pv \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('memberPV').value) || 0;  
            member.bv \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('memberBV').value) || 0;  
            member.vcsCompliant \= document.getElementById('vcsCompliance').checked;  
              
            updateOrgChart();  
            calculateAllIncome();  
            calculateAllIncentives();  
        });

        document.getElementById('deleteMember').addEventListener('click', deleteMember);  
        document.getElementById('deleteGroup').addEventListener('click', deleteGroup);  
        document.getElementById('addDownline').addEventListener('click', addDownlineMember);

        document.getElementById('switchPerspective').addEventListener('click', function() {  
            if (\!currentSelectedNode || currentSelectedNode \=== 'root') return;  
              
            // Switch perspective to selected member  
            alert(\`Switching to ${businessData.members\[currentSelectedNode\].name || 'IBO'}'s perspective \- Feature coming in next update\!\`);  
        });

        document.getElementById('expandAll').addEventListener('click', function() {  
            // Expand all functionality  
            updateOrgChart();  
        });

        document.getElementById('collapseAll').addEventListener('click', function() {  
            // Collapse all functionality  
            updateOrgChart();  
        });

        document.getElementById('monthSelector').addEventListener('change', function() {  
            const selectedMonth \= this.value;  
            // Save current structure to selected month  
            businessData.monthlyData\[selectedMonth\] \= JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(businessData.members));  
              
            // Update multi-month planning  
            updateMonthTimeline();  
        });

        function updateMonthTimeline() {  
            const timeline \= document.getElementById('monthTimeline');  
            timeline.innerHTML \= '';  
              
            Object.keys(businessData.monthlyData).forEach(month \=\> {  
                const monthCard \= document.createElement('div');  
                monthCard.className \= 'bg-white border-2 border-blue-200 rounded-lg p-3 min-w-48';  
                monthCard.innerHTML \= \`  
                    \<h5 class="font-bold text-gray-800 mb-2"\>${month}\</h5\>  
                    \<div class="text-xs space-y-1"\>  
                        \<div\>Total PV: ${Object.values(businessData.monthlyData\[month\]).reduce((sum, m) \=\> sum \+ (m.pv || 0), 0)}\</div\>  
                        \<div\>Total BV: ${Object.values(businessData.monthlyData\[month\]).reduce((sum, m) \=\> sum \+ (m.bv || 0), 0).toFixed(0)}\</div\>  
                        \<div\>Members: ${Object.keys(businessData.monthlyData\[month\]).length}\</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \`;  
                timeline.appendChild(monthCard);  
            });  
        }

        document.getElementById('applyStructure').addEventListener('click', function() {  
            if (\!document.getElementById('applyToMultiple').checked) return;  
              
            const checkboxes \= document.querySelectorAll('\#monthSelector2 input\[type="checkbox"\]:checked');  
            checkboxes.forEach(cb \=\> {  
                const monthLabel \= cb.parentNode.textContent.trim();  
                businessData.monthlyData\[monthLabel\] \= JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(businessData.members));  
            });  
              
            updateMonthTimeline();  
            calculateMultiMonthProjections();  
        });

        function calculateMultiMonthProjections() {  
            const monthCount \= Object.keys(businessData.monthlyData).length;  
            const currentMonthlyIncome \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('monthlyIncome').textContent.replace('$', '') || 0);  
            const totalProjected \= currentMonthlyIncome \* monthCount;  
            const average \= monthCount \> 0 ? totalProjected / monthCount : 0;  
              
            document.getElementById('selectedMonthsCount').textContent \= monthCount;  
            document.getElementById('totalProjectedIncome').textContent \= '$' \+ totalProjected.toFixed(0);  
            document.getElementById('averageMonthlyIncome').textContent \= '$' \+ average.toFixed(0);  
        }

        // Initialize Application  
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {  
            initializeOrgChart();  
            selectNode('root');  
            calculateAllIncome();  
            calculateAllIncentives();  
              
            // Auto-calculation on PV changes  
            document.getElementById('memberPV').addEventListener('input', function() {  
                setTimeout(() \=\> {  
                    if (currentSelectedNode && businessData.members\[currentSelectedNode\]) {  
                        businessData.members\[currentSelectedNode\].pv \= parseFloat(this.value) || 0;  
                        businessData.members\[currentSelectedNode\].bv \= (parseFloat(this.value) || 0\) \* 3.43;  
                        calculateAllIncome();  
                        calculateAllIncentives();  
                    }  
                }, 300);  
            });  
        });  
    \</script\>  
\</body\>  
\</html\>
