                            \<label class="flex items-center text-sm"\>\<input type="checkbox" class="month-checkbox mr-1" value="2025-12"\> Dec\</label\>  
                        \</div\>

                        \<label class="flex items-center mb-4"\>  
                            \<input type="checkbox" id="applyCurrentStructure" class="mr-2"\>  
                            \<span class="text-sm"\>Apply current Visual Builder structure to selected months\</span\>  
                        \</label\>

                        \<button class="w-full bg-blue-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-md hover:bg-blue-600 transition-colors" onclick="calculateMultiMonth()"\>  
                            \<i class="fas fa-calculator mr-2"\>\</i\>Calculate Multi-Month Income  
                        \</button\>  
                    \</div\>

                    \<\!-- Results \--\>  
                    \<div\>  
                        \<h3 class="text-lg font-semibold mb-4"\>Income Projections\</h3\>  
                        \<div id="multiMonthResults" class="space-y-4"\>  
                            \<div class="bg-gray-100 p-4 rounded-lg text-center"\>  
                                \<p class="text-gray-600"\>Select months and calculate to see projections\</p\>  
                            \</div\>  
                        \</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
            \</div\>  
        \</div\>

        \<\!-- Analytics Tab \--\>  
        \<div id="analytics" class="tab-content print-friendly"\>  
            \<div class="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-lg p-6"\>  
                \<h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800 mb-6"\>  
                    \<i class="fas fa-chart-line mr-2"\>\</i\>Performance Analytics  
                \</h2\>  
                  
                \<div class="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6"\>  
                    \<div\>  
                        \<h3 class="text-lg font-semibold mb-4"\>Income Trend\</h3\>  
                        \<canvas id="incomeChart" style="height: 300px;"\>\</canvas\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<div\>  
                        \<h3 class="text-lg font-semibold mb-4"\>Team Performance\</h3\>  
                        \<canvas id="teamChart" style="height: 300px;"\>\</canvas\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
            \</div\>  
        \</div\>

        \<\!-- Incentives Tab \--\>  
        \<div id="incentives" class="tab-content print-friendly"\>  
            \<div class="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-lg p-6"\>  
                \<h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800 mb-6"\>  
                    \<i class="fas fa-trophy mr-2"\>\</i\>Incentives & Bonuses  
                \</h2\>

                \<div class="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6"\>  
                    \<\!-- Auto-Calculated Incentives \--\>  
                    \<div\>  
                        \<h3 class="text-lg font-semibold mb-4"\>Auto-Calculated Incentives\</h3\>  
                        \<div id="autoIncentives" class="space-y-3"\>  
                            \<\!-- Auto-calculated incentives will be populated here \--\>  
                        \</div\>  
                    \</div\>

                    \<\!-- Manual Override \--\>  
                    \<div\>  
                        \<h3 class="text-lg font-semibold mb-4"\>Manual Bonuses & Overrides\</h3\>  
                        \<div class="space-y-4"\>  
                            \<div\>  
                                \<label class="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1"\>Additional Bonus Name\</label\>  
                                \<input type="text" id="bonusName" placeholder="e.g., Special Recognition Bonus" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"\>  
                            \</div\>  
                            \<div\>  
                                \<label class="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1"\>Amount\</label\>  
                                \<input type="number" id="bonusAmount" placeholder="Enter amount" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"\>  
                            \</div\>  
                            \<div\>  
                                \<label class="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1"\>Apply to Months\</label\>  
                                \<input type="text" id="bonusMonths" placeholder="e.g., January, February" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"\>  
                            \</div\>  
                            \<button class="w-full bg-green-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-md hover:bg-green-600 transition-colors" onclick="addManualBonus()"\>  
                                \<i class="fas fa-plus mr-2"\>\</i\>Add Manual Bonus  
                            \</button\>  
                        \</div\>

                        \<div class="mt-6"\>  
                            \<h4 class="font-semibold mb-2"\>Manual Bonuses Added\</h4\>  
                            \<div id="manualBonuses" class="space-y-2"\>  
                                \<\!-- Manual bonuses will be listed here \--\>  
                            \</div\>  
                        \</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
            \</div\>  
        \</div\>

        \<\!-- Reports Tab \--\>  
        \<div id="reports" class="tab-content print-friendly"\>  
            \<div class="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-lg p-6"\>  
                \<h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800 mb-6"\>  
                    \<i class="fas fa-file-alt mr-2"\>\</i\>Business Reports  
                \</h2\>

                \<div class="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6"\>  
                    \<div\>  
                        \<h3 class="text-lg font-semibold mb-4"\>Quick Reports\</h3\>  
                        \<div class="space-y-3"\>  
                            \<button class="w-full bg-blue-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-md hover:bg-blue-600 transition-colors text-left" onclick="generateOrgChartReport()"\>  
                                \<i class="fas fa-sitemap mr-2"\>\</i\>Organization Structure Report  
                            \</button\>  
                            \<button class="w-full bg-green-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-md hover:bg-green-600 transition-colors text-left" onclick="generateIncomeReport()"\>  
                                \<i class="fas fa-dollar-sign mr-2"\>\</i\>Income Projection Report  
                            \</button\>  
                            \<button class="w-full bg-purple-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-md hover:bg-purple-600 transition-colors text-left" onclick="generateVCSComplianceReport()"\>  
                                \<i class="fas fa-check-circle mr-2"\>\</i\>VCS Compliance Report  
                            \</button\>  
                            \<button class="w-full bg-orange-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-md hover:bg-orange-600 transition-colors text-left" onclick="generateIncentiveReport()"\>  
                                \<i class="fas fa-trophy mr-2"\>\</i\>Incentives & Bonuses Report  
                            \</button\>  
                        \</div\>  
                    \</div\>

                    \<div\>  
                        \<h3 class="text-lg font-semibold mb-4"\>Report Preview\</h3\>  
                        \<div id="reportPreview" class="bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-lg min-h-64 text-sm"\>  
                            \<p class="text-gray-600 text-center"\>Select a report to preview\</p\>  
                        \</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
            \</div\>  
        \</div\>  
    \</div\>

    \<script\>  
        // Global variables  
        let currentSelectedMember \= null;  
        let organizationData \= {  
            root: {  
                id: 'root',  
                name: 'You',  
                pv: 150,  
                bv: 514.5,  
                vcsCompliant: true,  
                goal: 25,  
                children: \[\]  
            }  
        };  
        let monthlyData \= {};  
        let manualBonuses \= \[\];

        // Performance bonus schedule  
        const bonusSchedule \= \[  
            { min: 7500, max: Infinity, bonus: 25 },  
            { min: 6000, max: 7499, bonus: 23 },  
            { min: 4000, max: 5999, bonus: 21 },  
            { min: 2500, max: 3999, bonus: 18 },  
            { min: 1500, max: 2499, bonus: 15 },  
            { min: 1000, max: 1499, bonus: 12 },  
            { min: 600, max: 999, bonus: 9 },  
            { min: 300, max: 599, bonus: 6 },  
            { min: 100, max: 299, bonus: 3 },  
            { min: 0, max: 99, bonus: 0 }  
        \];

        // Tab management  
        function showTab(tabName) {  
            // Hide all tab contents  
            const tabContents \= document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content');  
            tabContents.forEach(content \=\> content.classList.remove('active'));  
              
            // Remove active class from all tab buttons  
            const tabButtons \= document.querySelectorAll('.tab-button');  
            tabButtons.forEach(button \=\> button.classList.remove('active'));  
              
            // Show selected tab and mark button as active  
            document.getElementById(tabName).classList.add('active');  
            event.target.classList.add('active');  
              
            // Initialize charts if analytics tab is selected  
            if (tabName \=== 'analytics') {  
                setTimeout(initCharts, 100);  
            }  
        }

        // Initialize the application  
        function init() {  
            loadData();  
            renderOrgChart();  
            updateIncomeDisplay();  
            calculateAutoIncentives();  
              
            // Set current month in dropdown  
            const currentDate \= new Date();  
            const currentMonthValue \= \`${currentDate.getFullYear()}-${String(currentDate.getMonth() \+ 1).padStart(2, '0')}\`;  
            document.getElementById('currentMonth').value \= currentMonthValue;  
        }

        // Update BV when PV changes  
        function updateMemberBV() {  
            const pv \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('memberPV').value) || 0;  
            const bv \= pv \* 3.43; // Official PV to BV ratio  
            document.getElementById('memberBV').value \= bv.toFixed(2);  
        }

        // Update VCS status warning  
        function updateVCSStatus() {  
            const vcsCompliant \= document.getElementById('vcsCompliant').checked;  
            const warning \= document.getElementById('vcsWarning');  
              
            if (vcsCompliant) {  
                warning.classList.add('hidden');  
            } else {  
                warning.classList.remove('hidden');  
            }  
        }

        // Save member data  
        function saveMember() {  
            if (\!currentSelectedMember) return;  
              
            const member \= findMemberById(organizationData.root, currentSelectedMember);  
            if (\!member) return;  
              
            member.name \= document.getElementById('memberName').value || member.name;  
            member.pv \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('memberPV').value) || 0;  
            member.bv \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('memberBV').value) || 0;  
            member.goal \= parseInt(document.getElementById('memberGoal').value) || 3;  
            member.vcsCompliant \= document.getElementById('vcsCompliant').checked;  
              
            saveData();  
            renderOrgChart();  
            updateIncomeDisplay();  
            calculateAutoIncentives();  
        }

        // Delete individual member (move their downline up)  
        function deleteMember() {  
            if (\!currentSelectedMember || currentSelectedMember \=== 'root') return;  
              
            if (confirm('Delete this member? Their downline will move up to their upline.')) {  
                deleteMemberById(organizationData.root, currentSelectedMember, false);  
                currentSelectedMember \= null;  
                clearMemberDetails();  
                saveData();  
                renderOrgChart();  
                updateIncomeDisplay();  
                calculateAutoIncentives();  
            }  
        }

        // Delete member with entire group  
        function deleteWithGroup() {  
            if (\!currentSelectedMember || currentSelectedMember \=== 'root') return;  
              
            if (confirm('Delete this member and their entire group?')) {  
                deleteMemberById(organizationData.root, currentSelectedMember, true);  
                currentSelectedMember \= null;  
                clearMemberDetails();  
                saveData();  
                renderOrgChart();  
                updateIncomeDisplay();  
                calculateAutoIncentives();  
            }  
        }

        // Add new team member  
        function addTeamMember(parentId) {  
            const parent \= findMemberById(organizationData.root, parentId);  
            if (\!parent) return;  
              
            const newId \= 'member\_' \+ Date.now();  
            const newMember \= {  
                id: newId,  
                name: \`New IBO\`,  
                pv: 100,  
                bv: 343,  
                vcsCompliant: true,  
                goal: 3,  
                children: \[\]  
            };  
              
            parent.children.push(newMember);  
            saveData();  
            renderOrgChart();  
            updateIncomeDisplay();  
            calculateAutoIncentives();  
        }

        // Render organization chart  
        function renderOrgChart() {  
            const container \= document.getElementById('orgNodes');  
            const svg \= document.getElementById('orgSvg');  
              
            container.innerHTML \= '';  
            svg.innerHTML \= '';  
              
            renderNode(organizationData.root, container, svg, 0, 0, 300);  
        }

        // Render individual node  
        function renderNode(member, container, svg, level, index, parentX \= 300\) {  
            const nodeWidth \= 120;  
            const nodeHeight \= 100;  
            const levelHeight \= 150;  
            const siblingSpacing \= 150;  
              
            // Calculate position  
            const childrenCount \= member.children.length;  
            const totalWidth \= childrenCount \* siblingSpacing;  
            const startX \= parentX \- totalWidth / 2;  
            const x \= level \=== 0 ? parentX : startX \+ (index \* siblingSpacing);  
            const y \= level \* levelHeight \+ 50;  
              
            // Create node element  
            const nodeDiv \= document.createElement('div');  
            nodeDiv.className \= \`member-node absolute bg-white rounded-xl shadow-lg p-3 text-center border-2 ${member.vcsCompliant ? 'vcs-compliant' : 'vcs-non-compliant'}\`;  
            nodeDiv.style.left \= (x \- nodeWidth / 2\) \+ 'px';  
            nodeDiv.style.top \= y \+ 'px';  
            nodeDiv.style.width \= nodeWidth \+ 'px';  
            nodeDiv.style.height \= nodeHeight \+ 'px';  
              
            // Calculate performance bonus  
            const bonusPercent \= getBonusPercent(member.pv);  
            const effectiveBV \= member.vcsCompliant ? member.bv : member.bv \* 0.7; // Prorate if not VCS compliant  
              
            nodeDiv.innerHTML \= \`  
                \<div class="text-xs font-semibold text-gray-800"\>${member.name}\</div\>  
                \<div class="text-xs text-blue-600 mt-1"\>${bonusPercent}%\</div\>  
                \<div class="text-xs text-gray-600"\>PV: ${member.pv}\</div\>  
                \<div class="text-xs text-gray-600"\>BV: ${effectiveBV.toFixed(0)}\</div\>  
                \<div class="text-xs ${member.vcsCompliant ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-red-600'} mt-1"\>  
                    ${member.vcsCompliant ? '‚úì VCS' : '‚ö† VCS'}  
                \</div\>  
                ${level \=== 0 ? '' : \`  
                \<button class="absolute \-bottom-2 \-right-2 bg-red-500 text-white rounded-full w-5 h-5 text-xs" onclick="deleteMemberById('${member.id}')"\>-\</button\>  
                \`}  
                \<button class="absolute \-bottom-2 \-left-2 bg-blue-500 text-white rounded-full w-5 h-5 text-xs" onclick="addTeamMember('${member.id}')"\>+\</button\>  
            \`;  
              
            nodeDiv.onclick \= (e) \=\> {  
                e.stopPropagation();  
                selectMember(member.id);  
            };  
              
            container.appendChild(nodeDiv);  
              
            // Draw connection lines to children  
            member.children.forEach((child, childIndex) \=\> {  
                const childX \= x \- (childrenCount \* siblingSpacing) / 2 \+ (childIndex \* siblingSpacing);  
                const childY \= y \+ levelHeight;  
                  
                // Draw line  
                const line \= document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'line');  
                line.setAttribute('x1', x);  
                line.setAttribute('y1', y \+ nodeHeight);  
                line.setAttribute('x2', childX);  
                line.setAttribute('y2', childY);  
                line.className \= 'connection-line';  
                svg.appendChild(line);  
                  
                // Render child node  
                renderNode(child, container, svg, level \+ 1, childIndex, x);  
            });  
        }

        // Select member for editing  
        function selectMember(memberId) {  
            currentSelectedMember \= memberId;  
            const member \= findMemberById(organizationData.root, memberId);  
            if (\!member) return;  
              
            // Populate member details form  
            document.getElementById('memberName').value \= member.name || '';  
            document.getElementById('memberPV').value \= member.pv || 0;  
            document.getElementById('memberBV').value \= member.bv || 0;  
            document.getElementById('memberGoal').value \= member.goal || 3;  
            document.getElementById('vcsCompliant').checked \= member.vcsCompliant \!== false;  
              
            updateVCSStatus();  
        }

        // Clear member details  
        function clearMemberDetails() {  
            document.getElementById('memberName').value \= '';  
            document.getElementById('memberPV').value \= '';  
            document.getElementById('memberBV').value \= '';  
            document.getElementById('memberGoal').value \= '3';  
            document.getElementById('vcsCompliant').checked \= false;  
        }

        // Find member by ID  
        function findMemberById(root, id) {  
            if (root.id \=== id) return root;  
              
            for (let child of root.children || \[\]) {  
                const found \= findMemberById(child, id);  
                if (found) return found;  
            }  
              
            return null;  
        }

        // Delete member by ID  
        function deleteMemberById(root, id, deleteGroup \= true) {  
            if (\!root.children) return false;  
              
            for (let i \= 0; i \< root.children.length; i++) {  
                if (root.children\[i\].id \=== id) {  
                    const deletedMember \= root.children\[i\];  
                    if (\!deleteGroup && deletedMember.children) {  
                        // Move children up to parent  
                        root.children.splice(i, 1, ...deletedMember.children);  
                    } else {  
                        // Delete entire group  
                        root.children.splice(i, 1);  
                    }  
                    return true;  
                }  
                  
                if (deleteMemberById(root.children\[i\], id, deleteGroup)) {  
                    return true;  
                }  
            }  
              
            return false;  
        }

        // Get bonus percentage based on PV  
        function getBonusPercent(pv) {  
            for (let bracket of bonusSchedule) {  
                if (pv \>= bracket.min && pv \<= bracket.max) {  
                    return bracket.bonus;  
                }  
            }  
            return 0;  
        }

        // Calculate total organization stats  
        function calculateTotalStats(member \= organizationData.root) {  
            let totalPV \= member.pv || 0;  
            let totalBV \= (member.vcsCompliant \!== false ? member.bv : member.bv \* 0.7) || 0;  
            let qualifiedMembers \= 0;  
              
            if (member.vcsCompliant \!== false) qualifiedMembers++;  
              
            for (let child of member.children || \[\]) {  
                const childStats \= calculateTotalStats(child);  
                totalPV \+= childStats.totalPV;  
                totalBV \+= childStats.totalBV;  
                qualifiedMembers \+= childStats.qualifiedMembers;  
            }  
              
            return { totalPV, totalBV, qualifiedMembers };  
        }

        // Update income display  
        function updateIncomeDisplay() {  
            const stats \= calculateTotalStats();  
            const bonusPercent \= getBonusPercent(stats.totalPV);  
            const performanceBonus \= stats.totalBV \* (bonusPercent / 100);  
              
            // Calculate leadership and depth bonuses (simplified)  
            let leadershipBonus \= 0;  
            const rootBonusPercent \= getBonusPercent(organizationData.root.pv);  
              
            for (let child of organizationData.root.children || \[\]) {  
                const childStats \= calculateTotalStats(child);  
                const childBonusPercent \= getBonusPercent(childStats.totalPV);  
                const differential \= (rootBonusPercent \- childBonusPercent) / 100;  
                if (differential \> 0\) {  
                    leadershipBonus \+= childStats.totalBV \* differential;  
                }  
            }  
              
            const totalIncome \= performanceBonus \+ leadershipBonus;  
              
            document.getElementById('monthlyIncome').textContent \= '$' \+ Math.round(totalIncome);  
            document.getElementById('performanceBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ Math.round(performanceBonus);  
            document.getElementById('leadershipBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ Math.round(leadershipBonus);  
            document.getElementById('totalPV').textContent \= Math.round(stats.totalPV);  
        }

        // Calculate auto incentives  
        function calculateAutoIncentives() {  
            const stats \= calculateTotalStats();  
            const autoIncentivesDiv \= document.getElementById('autoIncentives');  
              
            if (\!autoIncentivesDiv) return;  
              
            let incentives \= \[\];  
              
            // Check for Platinum qualification (simplified)  
            const totalPV \= stats.totalPV;  
            const qualifiedLegs \= organizationData.root.children.filter(child \=\> {  
                const childStats \= calculateTotalStats(child);  
                return childStats.totalPV \>= 2500; // 18% level  
            }).length;  
              
            if (totalPV \>= 7500 && qualifiedLegs \>= 3\) {  
                incentives.push({  
                    name: 'Platinum Qualification Incentive',  
                    amount: 1500,  
                    description: 'First-time Platinum qualification bonus'  
                });  
            }  
              
            if (totalPV \>= 7500 && qualifiedLegs \>= 6\) {  
                incentives.push({  
                    name: 'Founders Platinum Potential',  
                    amount: 3500,  
                    description: 'Projected Founders Platinum bonus'  
                });  
            }  
              
            // Ruby bonus  
            if (totalPV \>= 15000\) {  
                incentives.push({  
                    name: 'Ruby Bonus',  
                    amount: Math.round(stats.totalBV \* 0.02),  
                    description: '2% of Ruby BV (15,000+ PV)'  
                });  
            }  
              
            autoIncentivesDiv.innerHTML \= incentives.length \> 0   
                ? incentives.map(incentive \=\> \`  
                    \<div class="incentive-earned border border-green-300 rounded-lg p-3"\>  
                        \<div class="font-semibold text-green-800"\>${incentive.name}\</div\>  
                        \<div class="text-green-600"\>$${incentive.amount}\</div\>  
                        \<div class="text-xs text-gray-600"\>${incentive.description}\</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \`).join('')  
                : '\<div class="text-gray-500 text-sm"\>No automatic incentives qualified yet\</div\>';  
        }

        // Add manual bonus  
        function addManualBonus() {  
            const name \= document.getElementById('bonusName').value;  
            const amount \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('bonusAmount').value);  
            const months \= document.getElementById('bonusMonths').value;  
              
            if (\!name || \!amount) {  
                alert('Please enter both bonus name and amount');  
                return;  
            }  
              
            manualBonuses.push({ name, amount, months });  
              
            // Clear form  
            document.getElementById('bonusName').value \= '';  
            document.getElementById('bonusAmount').value \= '';  
            document.getElementById('bonusMonths').value \= '';  
              
            renderManualBonuses();  
            saveData();  
        }

        // Render manual bonuses  
        function renderManualBonuses() {  
            const container \= document.getElementById('manualBonuses');  
            if (\!container) return;  
              
            container.innerHTML \= manualBonuses.map((bonus, index) \=\> \`  
                \<div class="bg-gray-100 rounded-lg p-2 flex justify-between items-center"\>  
                    \<div\>  
                        \<div class="font-medium"\>${bonus.name}\</div\>  
                        \<div class="text-sm text-gray-600"\>$${bonus.amount} \- ${bonus.months || 'All months'}\</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                    \<button class="text-red-500 text-sm" onclick="removeManualBonus(${index})"\>Remove\</button\>  
                \</div\>  
            \`).join('');  
        }

        // Remove manual bonus  
        function removeManualBonus(index) {  
            manualBonuses.splice(index, 1);  
            renderManualBonuses();  
            saveData();  
        }

        // Multi-month calculations  
        function calculateMultiMonth() {  
            const selectedMonths \= Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.month-checkbox:checked')).map(cb \=\> cb.value);  
            const applyStructure \= document.getElementById('applyCurrentStructure').checked;  
              
            if (selectedMonths.length \=== 0\) {  
                alert('Please select at least one month');  
                return;  
            }  
              
            const results \= document.getElementById('multiMonthResults');  
            let totalIncome \= 0;  
            let monthlyBreakdown \= \[\];  
              
            selectedMonths.forEach(month \=\> {  
                const stats \= calculateTotalStats();  
                const bonusPercent \= getBonusPercent(stats.totalPV);  
                const performanceBonus \= stats.totalBV \* (bonusPercent / 100);  
                  
                let leadershipBonus \= 0;  
                const rootBonusPercent \= getBonusPercent(organizationData.root.pv);  
                  
                for (let child of organizationData.root.children || \[\]) {  
                    const childStats \= calculateTotalStats(child);  
                    const childBonusPercent \= getBonusPercent(childStats.totalPV);  
                    const differential \= (rootBonusPercent \- childBonusPercent) / 100;  
                    if (differential \> 0\) {  
                        leadershipBonus \+= childStats.totalBV \* differential;  
                    }  
                }  
                  
                const monthlyIncome \= performanceBonus \+ leadershipBonus;  
                totalIncome \+= monthlyIncome;  
                  
                monthlyBreakdown.push({  
                    month: month,  
                    income: monthlyIncome,  
                    pv: stats.totalPV  
                });  
            });  
              
            results.innerHTML \= \`  
                \<div class="bg-green-100 p-4 rounded-lg"\>  
                    \<h4 class="font-bold text-green-800"\>Total Projected Income\</h4\>  
                    \<div class="text-2xl font-bold text-green-600"\>$${Math.round(totalIncome)}\</div\>  
                    \<div class="text-sm text-green-700"\>Over ${selectedMonths.length} months\</div\>  
                \</div\>  
                \<div class="space-y-2"\>  
                    \<h4 class="font-semibold"\>Monthly Breakdown\</h4\>  
                    ${monthlyBreakdown.map(month \=\> \`  
                        \<div class="bg-gray-100 p-2 rounded flex justify-between"\>  
                            \<span\>${month.month}\</span\>  
                            \<span\>$${Math.round(month.income)} (${Math.round(month.pv)} PV)\</span\>  
                        \</div\>  
                    \`).join('')}  
                \</div\>  
            \`;  
        }

        // Initialize charts  
        function initCharts() {  
            // Income trend chart  
            const incomeCtx \= document.getElementById('incomeChart');  
            if (incomeCtx) {  
                new Chart(incomeCtx, {  
                    type: 'line',  
                    data: {  
                        labels: \['Jan', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Apr', 'May', 'Jun'\],  
                        datasets: \[{  
                            label: 'Monthly Income',  
                            data: \[1200, 1500, 1800, 2200, 2800, 3200\],  
                            borderColor: '\#4F46E5',  
                            backgroundColor: 'rgba(79, 70, 229, 0.1)',  
                            tension: 0.4  
                        }\]  
                    },  
                    options: {  
                        responsive: true,  
                        maintainAspectRatio: false,  
                        scales: {  
                            y: {  
                                beginAtZero: true  
                            }  
                        }  
                    }  
                });  
            }  
              
            // Team performance chart  
            const teamCtx \= document.getElementById('teamChart');  
            if (teamCtx) {  
                new Chart(teamCtx, {  
                    type: 'doughnut',  
                    data: {  
                        labels: \['VCS Compliant', 'Non-Compliant'\],  
                        datasets: \[{  
                            data: \[80, 20\],  
                            backgroundColor: \['\#10B981', '\#EF4444'\]  
                        }\]  
                    },  
                    options: {  
                        responsive: true,  
                        maintainAspectRatio: false  
                    }  
                });  
            }  
        }

        // Report generation functions  
        function generateOrgChartReport() {  
            const stats \= calculateTotalStats();  
            const reportPreview \= document.getElementById('reportPreview');  
              
            reportPreview.innerHTML \= \`  
                \<h3 class="font-bold mb-2"\>Organization Structure Report\</h3\>  
                \<div class="space-y-2"\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Total Team Members:\</strong\> ${countTotalMembers(organizationData.root) \- 1}\</p\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Total PV:\</strong\> ${Math.round(stats.totalPV)}\</p\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Total BV:\</strong\> ${Math.round(stats.totalBV)}\</p\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>VCS Compliant Members:\</strong\> ${stats.qualifiedMembers}\</p\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Performance Bonus Level:\</strong\> ${getBonusPercent(stats.totalPV)}%\</p\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Direct Frontline:\</strong\> ${organizationData.root.children.length}\</p\>  
                \</div\>  
            \`;  
        }  
          
        function generateIncomeReport() {  
            const stats \= calculateTotalStats();  
            const bonusPercent \= getBonusPercent(stats.totalPV);  
            const performanceBonus \= stats.totalBV \* (bonusPercent / 100);  
              
            let leadershipBonus \= 0;  
            const rootBonusPercent \= getBonusPercent(organizationData.root.pv);  
              
            for (let child of organizationData.root.children || \[\]) {  
                const childStats \= calculateTotalStats(child);  
                const childBonusPercent \= getBonusPercent(childStats.totalPV);  
                const differential \= (rootBonusPercent \- childBonusPercent) / 100;  
                if (differential \> 0\) {  
                    leadershipBonus \+= childStats.totalBV \* differential;  
                }  
            }  
              
            const totalIncome \= performanceBonus \+ leadershipBonus;  
              
            const reportPreview \= document.getElementById('reportPreview');  
            reportPreview.innerHTML \= \`  
                \<h3 class="font-bold mb-2"\>Income Projection Report\</h3\>  
                \<div class="space-y-2"\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Performance Bonus:\</strong\> $${Math.round(performanceBonus)}\</p\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Leadership Bonus:\</strong\> $${Math.round(leadershipBonus)}\</p\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Total Monthly Income:\</strong\> $${Math.round(totalIncome)}\</p\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Annual Projection:\</strong\> $${Math.round(totalIncome \* 12)}\</p\>  
                    \<hr class="my-2"\>  
                    \<p class="text-xs"\>Based on current organization structure and PV/BV levels\</p\>  
                \</div\>  
            \`;  
        }  
          
        function generateVCSComplianceReport() {  
            const reportPreview \= document.getElementById('reportPreview');  
            let compliantCount \= 0;  
            let totalCount \= 0;  
              
            function countCompliance(member) {  
                totalCount++;  
                if (member.vcsCompliant \!== false) compliantCount++;  
                  
                for (let child of member.children || \[\]) {  
                    countCompliance(child);  
                }  
            }  
              
            countCompliance(organizationData.root);  
              
            const complianceRate \= Math.round((compliantCount / totalCount) \* 100);  
              
            reportPreview.innerHTML \= \`  
                \<h3 class="font-bold mb-2"\>VCS Compliance Report\</h3\>  
                \<div class="space-y-2"\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Compliance Rate:\</strong\> ${complianceRate}%\</p\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Compliant Members:\</strong\> ${compliantCount}\</p\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Non-Compliant Members:\</strong\> ${totalCount \- compliantCount}\</p\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Total Members:\</strong\> ${totalCount}\</p\>  
                    \<hr class="my-2"\>  
                    \<p class="text-xs"\>VCS Requirement: 60% of PV from Verified Customer Sales\</p\>  
                    \<p class="text-xs"\>Customer Sales Requirement: 70% of PV from customer sales\</p\>  
                \</div\>  
            \`;  
        }  
          
        function generateIncentiveReport() {  
            const reportPreview \= document.getElementById('reportPreview');  
            const stats \= calculateTotalStats();  
            let qualifiedIncentives \= \[\];  
              
            // Check qualifications  
            if (stats.totalPV \>= 7500\) {  
                qualifiedIncentives.push('Platinum Level Qualified');  
            }  
            if (stats.totalPV \>= 15000\) {  
                qualifiedIncentives.push('Ruby Bonus Eligible');  
            }  
              
            const manualBonusTotal \= manualBonuses.reduce((total, bonus) \=\> total \+ bonus.amount, 0);  
              
            reportPreview.innerHTML \= \`  
                \<h3 class="font-bold mb-2"\>Incentives & Bonuses Report\</h3\>  
                \<div class="space-y-2"\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Qualified Incentives:\</strong\>\</p\>  
                    \<ul class="list-disc list-inside ml-4"\>  
                        ${qualifiedIncentives.map(incentive \=\> \`\<li class="text-sm"\>${incentive}\</li\>\`).join('')}  
                    \</ul\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Manual Bonuses Added:\</strong\> ${manualBonuses.length}\</p\>  
                    \<p\>\<strong\>Manual Bonus Total:\</strong\> $${manualBonusTotal}\</p\>  
                    \<hr class="my-2"\>  
                    \<p class="text-xs"\>Based on current performance levels and manual entries\</p\>  
                \</div\>  
            \`;  
        }  
          
        // Utility functions  
        function countTotalMembers(member) {  
            let count \= 1;  
            for (let child of member.children || \[\]) {  
                count \+= countTotalMembers(child);  
            }  
            return count;  
        }

        function expandAll() {  
            // Implementation for expand all functionality  
            renderOrgChart();  
        }

        function collapseAll() {  
            // Implementation for collapse all functionality  
            renderOrgChart();  
        }

        // Data persistence  
        function saveData() {  
            const data \= {  
                organizationData,  
                monthlyData,  
                manualBonuses  
            };  
            localStorage.setItem('amwayBusinessPlanner', JSON.stringify(data));  
        }

        function loadData() {  
            const savedData \= localStorage.getItem('amwayBusinessPlanner');  
            if (savedData) {  
                const data \= JSON.parse(savedData);  
                organizationData \= data.organizationData || organizationData;  
                monthlyData \= data.monthlyData || {};  
                manualBonuses \= data.manualBonuses || \[\];  
                renderManualBonuses();  
            }  
        }

        // Initialize the application when page loads  
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {  
            init();  
            selectMember('root'); // Select root by default  
        });  
    \</script\>  
\</body\>  
\</html\>

\<script\>  
// Global variables  
let businessData \= {  
    members: new Map(),  
    monthlyData: new Map(),  
    incentives: new Map(),  
    selectedMember: null  
};

const PV\_TO\_BV\_RATIO \= 3.43; // Official Amway ratio as of September 2024

// Performance bonus schedule (PV ranges to percentage)  
const PERFORMANCE\_BONUS\_SCHEDULE \= \[  
    { min: 7500, max: Infinity, percentage: 25 },  
    { min: 6000, max: 7499, percentage: 23 },  
    { min: 4000, max: 5999, percentage: 21 },  
    { min: 2500, max: 3999, percentage: 18 },  
    { min: 1500, max: 2499, percentage: 15 },  
    { min: 1000, max: 1499, percentage: 12 },  
    { min: 600, max: 999, percentage: 9 },  
    { min: 300, max: 599, percentage: 6 },  
    { min: 100, max: 299, percentage: 3 },  
    { min: 0, max: 99, percentage: 0 }  
\];

// Initialize app  
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {  
    loadBusinessData();  
    initializeEventListeners();  
    initializeCharts();  
    calculateTotals();  
      
    // Set you (root) default values  
    const yourPV \= 150;  
    const yourBV \= yourPV \* PV\_TO\_BV\_RATIO;  
    document.getElementById('yourPV').textContent \= yourPV;  
    document.getElementById('yourBV').textContent \= yourBV.toFixed(2);  
      
    // Save root member data  
    businessData.members.set('root', {  
        id: 'root',  
        name: 'You',  
        pv: yourPV,  
        bv: yourBV,  
        level: 0,  
        parent: null,  
        children: \[\],  
        goal: 25  
    });  
});

// Tab functionality  
document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(btn \=\> {  
    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {  
        const tabName \= this.dataset.tab;  
          
        // Update button states  
        document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(b \=\> {  
            b.classList.remove('border-blue-500', 'text-blue-600');  
            b.classList.add('text-gray-600');  
        });  
        this.classList.add('border-blue-500', 'text-blue-600');  
        this.classList.remove('text-gray-600');  
          
        // Show/hide content  
        document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(content \=\> {  
            content.classList.remove('active');  
        });  
        document.getElementById(tabName).classList.add('active');  
          
        // Update charts when analytics tab is opened  
        if (tabName \=== 'analytics') {  
            updateAllCharts();  
        }  
    });  
});

// Event listeners  
function initializeEventListeners() {  
    // Member form PV input \- auto-calculate BV  
    document.getElementById('memberPV').addEventListener('input', function() {  
        const pv \= parseFloat(this.value) || 0;  
        const bv \= pv \* PV\_TO\_BV\_RATIO;  
        document.getElementById('memberBV').value \= bv.toFixed(2);  
    });  
      
    // New member form PV input \- auto-calculate BV  
    document.getElementById('newMemberPV').addEventListener('input', function() {  
        const pv \= parseFloat(this.value) || 0;  
        const bv \= pv \* PV\_TO\_BV\_RATIO;  
        document.getElementById('newMemberBV').value \= bv.toFixed(2);  
    });  
      
    // Add member buttons  
    document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {  
        if (e.target.classList.contains('add-member-btn') || e.target.closest('.add-member-btn')) {  
            const btn \= e.target.classList.contains('add-member-btn') ? e.target : e.target.closest('.add-member-btn');  
            const level \= parseInt(btn.dataset.level);  
            const parent \= btn.dataset.parent;  
            showMemberModal(level, parent);  
        }  
    });  
      
    // Member node clicks  
    document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {  
        if (e.target.classList.contains('member-node') || e.target.closest('.member-node')) {  
            const node \= e.target.classList.contains('member-node') ? e.target : e.target.closest('.member-node');  
            if (node.dataset.memberId) {  
                selectMember(node.dataset.memberId);  
            }  
        }  
    });  
      
    // Save member  
    document.getElementById('saveMember').addEventListener('click', saveMemberDetails);  
      
    // Delete member  
    document.getElementById('deleteMember').addEventListener('click', function() {  
        if (businessData.selectedMember && businessData.selectedMember \!== 'root') {  
            deleteMember(businessData.selectedMember, false);  
        }  
    });  
      
    // Delete with group  
    document.getElementById('deleteWithGroup').addEventListener('click', function() {  
        if (businessData.selectedMember && businessData.selectedMember \!== 'root') {  
            deleteMember(businessData.selectedMember, true);  
        }  
    });  
      
    // New member form  
    document.getElementById('newMemberForm').addEventListener('submit', addNewMember);  
    document.getElementById('cancelMember').addEventListener('click', hideMemberModal);  
      
    // Month selection  
    document.querySelectorAll('.month-checkbox').forEach(checkbox \=\> {  
        checkbox.addEventListener('change', updateMultiMonthCalculations);  
    });  
      
    // Quick month selection buttons  
    document.getElementById('selectCurrentYear').addEventListener('click', function() {  
        document.querySelectorAll('.month-checkbox').forEach(cb \=\> {  
            cb.checked \= cb.value.startsWith('2024');  
        });  
        updateMultiMonthCalculations();  
    });  
      
    document.getElementById('selectNextYear').addEventListener('click', function() {  
        document.querySelectorAll('.month-checkbox').forEach(cb \=\> {  
            cb.checked \= cb.value.startsWith('2025');  
        });  
        updateMultiMonthCalculations();  
    });  
      
    document.getElementById('applyStructureToSelected').addEventListener('click', applyStructureToSelectedMonths);  
    document.getElementById('clearAllMonths').addEventListener('click', function() {  
        document.querySelectorAll('.month-checkbox').forEach(cb \=\> cb.checked \= false);  
        updateMultiMonthCalculations();  
    });  
      
    // Incentive checkboxes  
    document.querySelectorAll('.incentive-checkbox').forEach(checkbox \=\> {  
        checkbox.addEventListener('change', function() {  
            const amountInput \= this.parentNode.querySelector('.incentive-amount');  
            amountInput.disabled \= \!this.checked;  
            if (\!this.checked) {  
                amountInput.value \= '';  
            }  
            updateIncentiveTotals();  
        });  
    });  
      
    // Incentive amounts  
    document.querySelectorAll('.incentive-amount').forEach(input \=\> {  
        input.addEventListener('input', updateIncentiveTotals);  
    });  
      
    // Report generation  
    document.querySelectorAll('.generate-report-btn').forEach(btn \=\> {  
        btn.addEventListener('click', function() {  
            const reportType \= this.dataset.report;  
            generateReport(reportType);  
        });  
    });  
      
    // Expand/collapse org chart  
    document.getElementById('expandAll').addEventListener('click', function() {  
        document.querySelectorAll('.member-children').forEach(el \=\> {  
            el.classList.remove('hidden');  
        });  
    });  
      
    document.getElementById('collapseAll').addEventListener('click', function() {  
        document.querySelectorAll('.member-children').forEach(el \=\> {  
            if (\!el.parentNode.dataset.memberId \=== 'root') {  
                el.classList.add('hidden');  
            }  
        });  
    });  
}

// Member management functions  
function showMemberModal(level, parent) {  
    document.getElementById('memberModal').classList.remove('hidden');  
    document.getElementById('newMemberForm').dataset.level \= level;  
    document.getElementById('newMemberForm').dataset.parent \= parent;  
}

function hideMemberModal() {  
    document.getElementById('memberModal').classList.add('hidden');  
    document.getElementById('newMemberForm').reset();  
}

function addNewMember(e) {  
    e.preventDefault();  
      
    const form \= e.target;  
    const name \= document.getElementById('newMemberName').value;  
    const pv \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('newMemberPV').value) || 0;  
    const bv \= pv \* PV\_TO\_BV\_RATIO;  
    const level \= parseInt(form.dataset.level);  
    const parent \= form.dataset.parent;  
      
    const memberId \= 'member\_' \+ Date.now() \+ '\_' \+ Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9);  
      
    const memberData \= {  
        id: memberId,  
        name: name,  
        pv: pv,  
        bv: bv,  
        level: level,  
        parent: parent,  
        children: \[\],  
        goal: getPerformanceBonusLevel(pv)  
    };  
      
    businessData.members.set(memberId, memberData);  
      
    // Add to parent's children  
    if (parent \!== 'root') {  
        const parentMember \= businessData.members.get(parent);  
        if (parentMember) {  
            parentMember.children.push(memberId);  
        }  
    }  
      
    renderOrganizationChart();  
    calculateTotals();  
    saveBusinessData();  
    hideMemberModal();  
}

function selectMember(memberId) {  
    businessData.selectedMember \= memberId;  
    const member \= businessData.members.get(memberId);  
      
    if (member) {  
        document.getElementById('memberName').value \= member.name;  
        document.getElementById('memberPV').value \= member.pv;  
        document.getElementById('memberBV').value \= member.bv.toFixed(2);  
        document.getElementById('memberGoal').value \= member.goal;  
          
        // Highlight selected member  
        document.querySelectorAll('.member-node').forEach(node \=\> {  
            node.classList.remove('ring-4', 'ring-blue-500');  
        });  
          
        const selectedNode \= document.querySelector(\`\[data-member-id="${memberId}"\]\`);  
        if (selectedNode) {  
            selectedNode.classList.add('ring-4', 'ring-blue-500');  
        }  
    }  
}

function saveMemberDetails() {  
    if (\!businessData.selectedMember) return;  
      
    const member \= businessData.members.get(businessData.selectedMember);  
    if (member) {  
        member.name \= document.getElementById('memberName').value;  
        member.pv \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('memberPV').value) || 0;  
        member.bv \= member.pv \* PV\_TO\_BV\_RATIO;  
        member.goal \= parseInt(document.getElementById('memberGoal').value);  
          
        renderOrganizationChart();  
        calculateTotals();  
        saveBusinessData();  
    }  
}

function deleteMember(memberId, deleteGroup \= false) {  
    const member \= businessData.members.get(memberId);  
    if (\!member) return;  
      
    if (deleteGroup) {  
        // Delete member and all their children  
        deleteWithChildren(memberId);  
    } else {  
        // Delete member but move children up to parent  
        const children \= \[...member.children\];  
        const parent \= member.parent;  
          
        // Move children to parent  
        children.forEach(childId \=\> {  
            const child \= businessData.members.get(childId);  
            if (child) {  
                child.parent \= parent;  
                child.level \= member.level; // Move up one level  
            }  
        });  
          
        // Add children to parent's children array  
        if (parent && parent \!== 'root') {  
            const parentMember \= businessData.members.get(parent);  
            if (parentMember) {  
                parentMember.children \= parentMember.children.filter(id \=\> id \!== memberId);  
                parentMember.children.push(...children);  
            }  
        }  
          
        // Remove member  
        businessData.members.delete(memberId);  
    }  
      
    businessData.selectedMember \= null;  
    document.getElementById('memberForm').reset();  
    renderOrganizationChart();  
    calculateTotals();  
    saveBusinessData();  
}

function deleteWithChildren(memberId) {  
    const member \= businessData.members.get(memberId);  
    if (\!member) return;  
      
    // Recursively delete all children  
    member.children.forEach(childId \=\> {  
        deleteWithChildren(childId);  
    });  
      
    // Remove from parent's children array  
    if (member.parent && member.parent \!== 'root') {  
        const parent \= businessData.members.get(member.parent);  
        if (parent) {  
            parent.children \= parent.children.filter(id \=\> id \!== memberId);  
        }  
    }  
      
    // Delete member  
    businessData.members.delete(memberId);  
}

function renderOrganizationChart() {  
    const frontlineContainer \= document.getElementById('frontlineContainer');  
    frontlineContainer.innerHTML \= '';  
      
    // Get root member's children (frontline)  
    const rootMember \= businessData.members.get('root');  
    if (rootMember && rootMember.children.length \> 0\) {  
        rootMember.children.forEach(childId \=\> {  
            const memberElement \= createMemberElement(childId, 1);  
            frontlineContainer.appendChild(memberElement);  
        });  
    }  
}

function createMemberElement(memberId, level) {  
    const member \= businessData.members.get(memberId);  
    if (\!member) return null;  
      
    const bonusLevel \= getPerformanceBonusLevel(member.pv);  
    const memberDiv \= document.createElement('div');  
    memberDiv.className \= 'flex flex-col items-center';  
      
    memberDiv.innerHTML \= \`  
        \<div class="member-node bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-4 mb-4 max-w-xs cursor-pointer" data-member-id="${memberId}"\>  
            \<div class="text-center"\>  
                \<div class="w-12 h-12 bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-400 to-blue-600 rounded-full mx-auto mb-2 flex items-center justify-center"\>  
                    \<i class="fas fa-user text-white"\>\</i\>  
                \</div\>  
                \<h4 class="font-semibold text-gray-800 text-sm"\>${member.name}\</h4\>  
                \<div class="text-xs text-gray-600 mt-1"\>  
                    \<div\>PV: ${member.pv}\</div\>  
                    \<div\>BV: ${member.bv.toFixed(2)}\</div\>  
                    \<div class="text-green-600 font-semibold"\>${bonusLevel}%\</div\>  
                \</div\>  
            \</div\>  
            \<div class="flex justify-center mt-2 space-x-2"\>  
                \<button class="add-member-btn bg-green-500 text-white rounded-full w-6 h-6 flex items-center justify-center hover:bg-green-600 text-xs"   
                        data-level="${level \+ 1}" data-parent="${memberId}"\>  
                    \<i class="fas fa-plus text-xs"\>\</i\>  
                \</button\>  
            \</div\>  
        \</div\>  
    \`;  
      
    // Add children if any  
    if (member.children.length \> 0\) {  
        const childrenContainer \= document.createElement('div');  
        childrenContainer.className \= 'member-children flex flex-wrap justify-center gap-4 ml-8';  
          
        member.children.forEach(childId \=\> {  
            const childElement \= createMemberElement(childId, level \+ 1);  
            if (childElement) {  
                childrenContainer.appendChild(childElement);  
            }  
        });  
          
        memberDiv.appendChild(childrenContainer);  
    }  
      
    return memberDiv;  
}

function getPerformanceBonusLevel(pv) {  
    for (const bracket of PERFORMANCE\_BONUS\_SCHEDULE) {  
        if (pv \>= bracket.min && pv \<= bracket.max) {  
            return bracket.percentage;  
        }  
    }  
    return 0;  
}

function calculateTotals() {  
    let totalGroupPV \= 0;  
    let totalGroupBV \= 0;  
    let monthlyIncome \= 0;  
    let performanceBonus \= 0;  
    let leadershipBonus \= 0;  
      
    // Calculate total group volume  
    businessData.members.forEach(member \=\> {  
        totalGroupPV \+= member.pv;  
        totalGroupBV \+= member.bv;  
    });  
      
    // Calculate performance bonus  
    const bonusLevel \= getPerformanceBonusLevel(totalGroupPV);  
    performanceBonus \= (totalGroupBV \* bonusLevel) / 100;  
      
    // Calculate leadership bonus (simplified \- 4% of qualified legs)  
    const rootMember \= businessData.members.get('root');  
    if (rootMember) {  
        rootMember.children.forEach(childId \=\> {  
            const child \= businessData.members.get(childId);  
            if (child && getPerformanceBonusLevel(child.pv) \>= 6\) { // At least 6% level  
                const childGroupPV \= calculateGroupPV(childId);  
                const childGroupBV \= childGroupPV \* PV\_TO\_BV\_RATIO;  
                leadershipBonus \+= (childGroupBV \* 0.04); // 4% leadership bonus  
            }  
        });  
    }  
      
    monthlyIncome \= performanceBonus \+ leadershipBonus;  
      
    // Update UI  
    document.getElementById('totalGroupPV').textContent \= Math.round(totalGroupPV);  
    document.getElementById('monthlyIncome').textContent \= '$' \+ monthlyIncome.toFixed(0);  
    document.getElementById('performanceBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ performanceBonus.toFixed(0);  
    document.getElementById('leadershipBonus').textContent \= '$' \+ leadershipBonus.toFixed(0);  
}

function calculateGroupPV(memberId) {  
    const member \= businessData.members.get(memberId);  
    if (\!member) return 0;  
      
    let totalPV \= member.pv;  
      
    member.children.forEach(childId \=\> {  
        totalPV \+= calculateGroupPV(childId);  
    });  
      
    return totalPV;  
}

// Multi-month planning functions  
function updateMultiMonthCalculations() {  
    const selectedMonths \= Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.month-checkbox:checked'));  
    const monthCount \= selectedMonths.length;  
      
    // Get current monthly income  
    const monthlyIncome \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('monthlyIncome').textContent.replace('$', '').replace(',', '')) || 0;  
      
    const projectedIncome \= monthlyIncome \* monthCount;  
    const averageIncome \= monthCount \> 0 ? monthlyIncome : 0;  
      
    document.getElementById('selectedMonthsCount').textContent \= monthCount;  
    document.getElementById('multiMonthIncome').textContent \= '$' \+ projectedIncome.toLocaleString();  
    document.getElementById('averageMonthlyIncome').textContent \= '$' \+ averageIncome.toLocaleString();  
}

function applyStructureToSelectedMonths() {  
    const selectedMonths \= Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.month-checkbox:checked'));  
      
    selectedMonths.forEach(checkbox \=\> {  
        const monthKey \= checkbox.value;  
        businessData.monthlyData.set(monthKey, {  
            members: new Map(businessData.members),  
            structure: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(Array.from(businessData.members.entries())))  
        });  
    });  
      
    saveBusinessData();  
    alert(\`Applied current business structure to ${selectedMonths.length} selected months.\`);  
}

// Incentive tracking functions  
function updateIncentiveTotals() {  
    let total \= 0;  
      
    document.querySelectorAll('.incentive-checkbox:checked').forEach(checkbox \=\> {  
        const amountInput \= checkbox.parentNode.querySelector('.incentive-amount');  
        let amount \= 0;  
          
        if (amountInput.tagName \=== 'SELECT') {  
            amount \= parseFloat(amountInput.value) || 0;  
        } else {  
            amount \= parseFloat(amountInput.value) || 0;  
        }  
          
        total \+= amount;  
    });  
      
    document.getElementById('totalIncentives').textContent \= '$' \+ total.toLocaleString();  
}

// Chart initialization and updates  
function initializeCharts() {  
    // Performance Analytics Chart  
    const perfCtx \= document.getElementById('performanceChart').getContext('2d');  
    window.performanceChart \= new Chart(perfCtx, {  
        type: 'line',  
        data: {  
            labels: \['Jan', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Apr', 'May', 'Jun'\],  
            datasets: \[{  
                label: 'Monthly Income',  
                data: \[0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0\],  
                borderColor: 'rgb(59, 130, 246)',  
                backgroundColor: 'rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.1)',  
                tension: 0.4  
            }\]  
        },  
        options: {  
            responsive: true,  
            maintainAspectRatio: false,  
            plugins: {  
                legend: {  
                    display: true  
                }  
            },  
            scales: {  
                y: {  
                    beginAtZero: true,  
                    ticks: {  
                        callback: function(value) {  
                            return '$' \+ value.toLocaleString();  
                        }  
                    }  
                }  
            }  
        }  
    });  
      
    // Team Growth Chart  
    const teamCtx \= document.getElementById('teamGrowthChart').getContext('2d');  
    window.teamGrowthChart \= new Chart(teamCtx, {  
        type: 'bar',  
        data: {  
            labels: \['You', 'Level 1', 'Level 2', 'Level 3', 'Level 4+'\],  
            datasets: \[{  
                label: 'Team Members',  
                data: \[1, 0, 0, 0, 0\],  
                backgroundColor: 'rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.8)',  
                borderColor: 'rgb(34, 197, 94)',  
                borderWidth: 1  
            }\]  
        },  
        options: {  
            responsive: true,  
            maintainAspectRatio: false,  
            plugins: {  
                legend: {  
                    display: false  
                }  
            },  
            scales: {  
                y: {  
                    beginAtZero: true,  
                    ticks: {  
                        stepSize: 1  
                    }  
                }  
            }  
        }  
    });  
      
    // Income Breakdown Chart  
    const incomeCtx \= document.getElementById('incomeBreakdownChart').getContext('2d');  
    window.incomeBreakdownChart \= new Chart(incomeCtx, {  
        type: 'doughnut',  
        data: {  
            labels: \['Performance Bonus', 'Leadership Bonus', 'Depth Bonus', 'Incentives'\],  
            datasets: \[{  
                data: \[0, 0, 0, 0\],  
                backgroundColor: \[  
                    'rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.8)',  
                    'rgba(16, 185, 129, 0.8)',  
                    'rgba(245, 158, 11, 0.8)',  
                    'rgba(139, 92, 246, 0.8)'  
                \],  
                borderWidth: 2,  
                borderColor: '\#fff'  
            }\]  
        },  
        options: {  
            responsive: true,  
            maintainAspectRatio: false,  
            plugins: {  
                legend: {  
                    position: 'bottom'  
                }  
            }  
        }  
    });  
      
    // Goal Progress Chart  
    const goalCtx \= document.getElementById('goalProgressChart').getContext('2d');  
    window.goalProgressChart \= new Chart(goalCtx, {  
        type: 'radar',  
        data: {  
            labels: \['Personal Volume', 'Team Size', 'Income Goal', 'Leadership Development', 'Customer Base'\],  
            datasets: \[{  
                label: 'Current Progress',  
                data: \[20, 10, 15, 25, 30\],  
                borderColor: 'rgb(168, 85, 247)',  
                backgroundColor: 'rgba(168, 85, 247, 0.2)',  
                pointBackgroundColor: 'rgb(168, 85, 247)',  
                pointBorderColor: '\#fff',  
                pointHoverBackgroundColor: '\#fff',  
                pointHoverBorderColor: 'rgb(168, 85, 247)'  
            }\]  
        },  
        options: {  
            responsive: true,  
            maintainAspectRatio: false,  
            scales: {  
                r: {  
                    beginAtZero: true,  
                    max: 100  
                }  
            }  
        }  
    });  
}

function updateAllCharts() {  
    updatePerformanceChart();  
    updateTeamGrowthChart();  
    updateIncomeBreakdownChart();  
    updateGoalProgressChart();  
}

function updatePerformanceChart() {  
    // Generate sample data based on current income  
    const currentIncome \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('monthlyIncome').textContent.replace('$', '').replace(',', '')) || 0;  
    const data \= \[\];  
      
    for (let i \= 0; i \< 6; i++) {  
        // Add some variation to show growth trend  
        const variance \= (Math.random() \- 0.5) \* 0.3;  
        data.push(Math.max(0, currentIncome \* (0.7 \+ i \* 0.1 \+ variance)));  
    }  
      
    window.performanceChart.data.datasets\[0\].data \= data;  
    window.performanceChart.update();  
}

function updateTeamGrowthChart() {  
    const levels \= \[0, 0, 0, 0, 0\]; // \[You, Level 1, Level 2, Level 3, Level 4+\]  
    levels\[0\] \= 1; // You  
      
    businessData.members.forEach(member \=\> {  
        if (member.level \> 0 && member.level \< 5\) {  
            levels\[member.level\]++;  
        } else if (member.level \>= 5\) {  
            levels\[4\]++;  
        }  
    });  
      
    window.teamGrowthChart.data.datasets\[0\].data \= levels;  
    window.teamGrowthChart.update();  
}

function updateIncomeBreakdownChart() {  
    const performanceBonus \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('performanceBonus').textContent.replace('$', '').replace(',', '')) || 0;  
    const leadershipBonus \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('leadershipBonus').textContent.replace('$', '').replace(',', '')) || 0;  
    const incentives \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('totalIncentives').textContent.replace('$', '').replace(',', '')) || 0;  
    const depthBonus \= leadershipBonus \* 0.3; // Estimate depth bonus  
      
    window.incomeBreakdownChart.data.datasets\[0\].data \= \[  
        performanceBonus,  
        leadershipBonus,  
        depthBonus,  
        incentives  
    \];  
    window.incomeBreakdownChart.update();  
}

function updateGoalProgressChart() {  
    const totalPV \= parseInt(document.getElementById('totalGroupPV').textContent) || 0;  
    const teamSize \= businessData.members.size \- 1; // Exclude yourself  
    const currentIncome \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('monthlyIncome').textContent.replace('$', '').replace(',', '')) || 0;  
      
    // Calculate progress percentages (out of 100\)  
    const personalVolume \= Math.min(100, (totalPV / 1000\) \* 10); // Scale to 100  
    const teamSizeProgress \= Math.min(100, (teamSize / 50\) \* 100); // Target 50 team members  
    const incomeGoal \= Math.min(100, (currentIncome / 10000\) \* 100); // Target $10,000/month  
    const leadershipDev \= Math.min(100, (teamSize \* 10)); // Simple leadership metric  
    const customerBase \= Math.min(100, (personalVolume \* 2)); // Estimate customer base  
      
    window.goalProgressChart.data.datasets\[0\].data \= \[  
        personalVolume,  
        teamSizeProgress,  
        incomeGoal,  
        leadershipDev,  
        customerBase  
    \];  
    window.goalProgressChart.update();  
}

// Report generation  
function generateReport(reportType) {  
    const reportDisplay \= document.getElementById('reportDisplay');  
    const reportContent \= document.getElementById('reportContent');  
      
    let content \= '';  
      
    switch (reportType) {  
        case 'income':  
            content \= generateIncomeReport();  
            break;  
        case 'organization':  
            content \= generateOrganizationReport();  
            break;  
        case 'multimonth':  
            content \= generateMultiMonthReport();  
            break;  
    }  
      
    reportContent.innerHTML \= content;  
    reportDisplay.classList.remove('hidden');  
      
    // Scroll to report  
    reportDisplay.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });  
}

function generateIncomeReport() {  
    const monthlyIncome \= document.getElementById('monthlyIncome').textContent;  
    const performanceBonus \= document.getElementById('performanceBonus').textContent;  
    const leadershipBonus \= document.getElementById('leadershipBonus').textContent;  
    const totalGroupPV \= document.getElementById('totalGroupPV').textContent;  
    const totalIncentives \= document.getElementById('totalIncentives').textContent;  
      
    const annualIncome \= parseFloat(monthlyIncome.replace('$', '').replace(',', '')) \* 12;  
      
    return \`  
        \<div class="space-y-6"\>  
            \<h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800 text-center"\>Income Summary Report\</h2\>  
            \<div class="text-center text-sm text-gray-600"\>Generated on ${new Date().toLocaleDateString()}\</div\>  
              
            \<div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4"\>  
                \<div class="bg-blue-50 p-4 rounded-lg"\>  
                    \<h3 class="font-semibold text-blue-800"\>Monthly Performance\</h3\>  
                    \<div class="mt-2 space-y-2"\>  
                        \<div class="flex justify-between"\>  
                            \<span\>Performance Bonus:\</span\>  
                            \<span class="font-semibold"\>${performanceBonus}\</span\>  
                        \</div\>  
                        \<div class="flex justify-between"\>  
                            \<span\>Leadership Bonus:\</span\>  
                            \<span class="font-semibold"\>${leadershipBonus}\</span\>  
                        \</div\>  
                        \<div class="flex justify-between"\>  
                            \<span\>Additional Incentives:\</span\>  
                            \<span class="font-semibold"\>${totalIncentives}\</span\>  
                        \</div\>  
                        \<div class="border-t pt-2 flex justify-between"\>  
                            \<span class="font-bold"\>Total Monthly:\</span\>  
                            \<span class="font-bold text-green-600"\>${monthlyIncome}\</span\>  
                        \</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
                  
                \<div class="bg-green-50 p-4 rounded-lg"\>  
                    \<h3 class="font-semibold text-green-800"\>Annual Projection\</h3\>  
                    \<div class="mt-2 space-y-2"\>  
                        \<div class="flex justify-between"\>  
                            \<span\>Monthly Average:\</span\>  
                            \<span class="font-semibold"\>${monthlyIncome}\</span\>  
                        \</div\>  
                        \<div class="flex justify-between"\>  
                            \<span\>Annual Income:\</span\>  
                            \<span class="font-bold text-green-600"\>$${annualIncome.toLocaleString()}\</span\>  
                        \</div\>  
                        \<div class="flex justify-between"\>  
                            \<span\>Total Group PV:\</span\>  
                            \<span class="font-semibold"\>${totalGroupPV}\</span\>  
                        \</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
            \</div\>  
              
            \<div class="bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-lg"\>  
                \<h3 class="font-semibold text-gray-800 mb-3"\>Team Structure Summary\</h3\>  
                \<div class="text-sm space-y-1"\>  
                    \<div\>Total Team Members: ${businessData.members.size \- 1}\</div\>  
                    \<div\>Frontline Members: ${businessData.members.get('root')?.children?.length || 0}\</div\>  
                    \<div\>Performance Level: ${getPerformanceBonusLevel(parseInt(totalGroupPV))}%\</div\>  
                \</div\>  
            \</div\>  
        \</div\>  
    \`;  
}

function generateOrganizationReport() {  
    let content \= \`  
        \<div class="space-y-6"\>  
            \<h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800 text-center"\>Organization Structure Report\</h2\>  
            \<div class="text-center text-sm text-gray-600"\>Generated on ${new Date().toLocaleDateString()}\</div\>  
    \`;  
      
    content \+= '\<div class="space-y-4"\>';  
    content \+= generateMemberList('root', 0);  
    content \+= '\</div\>';  
    content \+= '\</div\>';  
      
    return content;  
}

function generateMemberList(memberId, level) {  
    const member \= businessData.members.get(memberId);  
    if (\!member) return '';  
      
    const indent \= '  '.repeat(level);  
    const bonusLevel \= getPerformanceBonusLevel(member.pv);  
      
    let content \= \`  
        \<div class="flex items-center space-x-4 p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-lg" style="margin-left: ${level \* 20}px;"\>  
            \<div class="flex-1"\>  
                \<h4 class="font-semibold"\>${member.name}\</h4\>  
                \<div class="text-sm text-gray-600"\>  
                    PV: ${member.pv} | BV: ${member.bv.toFixed(2)} | Level: ${bonusLevel}%  
                \</div\>  
            \</div\>  
        \</div\>  
    \`;  
      
    if (member.children.length \> 0\) {  
        member.children.forEach(childId \=\> {  
            content \+= generateMemberList(childId, level \+ 1);  
        });  
    }  
      
    return content;  
}

function generateMultiMonthReport() {  
    const selectedMonths \= Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.month-checkbox:checked'));  
    const monthlyIncome \= parseFloat(document.getElementById('monthlyIncome').textContent.replace('$', '').replace(',', '')) || 0;  
    const totalIncome \= monthlyIncome \* selectedMonths.length;  
      
    return \`  
        \<div class="space-y-6"\>  
            \<h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800 text-center"\>Multi-Month Analysis Report\</h2\>  
            \<div class="text-center text-sm text-gray-600"\>Generated on ${new Date().toLocaleDateString()}\</div\>  
              
            \<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4"\>  
                \<div class="bg-blue-50 p-4 rounded-lg"\>  
                    \<h3 class="font-semibold text-blue-800"\>Selected Period\</h3\>  
                    \<div class="mt-2"\>  
                        \<div\>Months Selected: ${selectedMonths.length}\</div\>  
                        \<div\>Period Income: $${totalIncome.toLocaleString()}\</div\>  
                        \<div\>Average/Month: $${monthlyIncome.toLocaleString()}\</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
                  
                \<div class="bg-green-50 p-4 rounded-lg"\>  
                    \<h3 class="font-semibold text-green-800"\>Performance Metrics\</h3\>  
                    \<div class="mt-2 text-sm"\>  
                        \<div\>Team Size: ${businessData.members.size \- 1}\</div\>  
                        \<div\>Total Group PV: ${document.getElementById('totalGroupPV').textContent}\</div\>  
                        \<div\>Performance Level: ${getPerformanceBonusLevel(parseInt(document.getElementById('totalGroupPV').textContent))}%\</div\>  
                    \</div\>  
                \</div\>  
            \</div\>  
              
            \<div class="bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-lg"\>  
                \<h3 class="font-semibold text-gray-800 mb-3"\>Selected Months:\</h3\>  
                \<div class="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2 text-sm"\>  
                    ${selectedMonths.map(cb \=\> \`\<div class="bg-white p-2 rounded"\>${cb.dataset.month}\</div\>\`).join('')}  
                \</div\>  
            \</div\>  
        \</div\>  
    \`;  
}

// Data persistence  
function saveBusinessData() {  
    const dataToSave \= {  
        members: Array.from(businessData.members.entries()),  
        monthlyData: Array.from(businessData.monthlyData.entries()),  
        incentives: Array.from(businessData.incentives.entries()),  
        lastSaved: new Date().toISOString()  
    };  
      
    localStorage.setItem('amwayBusinessData', JSON.stringify(dataToSave));  
}

function loadBusinessData() {  
    const savedData \= localStorage.getItem('amwayBusinessData');  
    if (savedData) {  
        try {  
            const parsed \= JSON.parse(savedData);  
            businessData.members \= new Map(parsed.members || \[\]);  
            businessData.monthlyData \= new Map(parsed.monthlyData || \[\]);  
            businessData.incentives \= new Map(parsed.incentives || \[\]);  
              
            // If no members exist, add default "You" member  
            if (\!businessData.members.has('root')) {  
                businessData.members.set('root', {  
                    id: 'root',  
                    name: 'You',  
                    pv: 150,  
                    bv: 150 \* PV\_TO\_BV\_RATIO,  
                    level: 0,  
                    parent: null,  
                    children: \[\],  
                    goal: 25  
                });  
            }  
              
            renderOrganizationChart();  
        } catch (error) {  
            console.error('Error loading business data:', error);  
            // Initialize with default data  
            businessData.members.set('root', {  
                id: 'root',  
                name: 'You',  
                pv: 150,  
                bv: 150 \* PV\_TO\_BV\_RATIO,  
                level: 0,  
                parent: null,  
                children: \[\],  
                goal: 25  
            });  
        }  
    }  
}

// Print functionality  
document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {  
    if (e.target.id \=== 'printReport') {  
        window.print();  
    }  
      
    if (e.target.id \=== 'shareReport') {  
        if (navigator.share) {  
            navigator.share({  
                title: 'Amway Business Plan Report',  
                text: 'Check out my Amway business analysis',  
                url: window.location.href  
            });  
        } else {  
            // Fallback \- copy URL to clipboard  
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(window.location.href).then(() \=\> {  
                alert('URL copied to clipboard\!');  
            });  
        }  
    }  
});  
\</script\>

\</html\>

        // Global variables  
        let currentScenario \= 'default';  
        let scenarios \= {  
            'default': {  
                name: 'Default Scenario',  
                organization: {

                        id: 'you',
